<span class="akn-akomaNtoso"><article class="akn-act" data-contains="originalVersion" data-name="act"><section class="akn-preface" id="preface"><span class="akn-p">Under the provisions of section 156(2) of the <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1996/constitution" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1996/constitution">Constitution of the Republic of South Africa, 1996</a>, the Bergrivier Municipality, enacts as follows:</span></section><span class="akn-body"><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_I" data-eId="chp_I"><h2>Chapter I<br>Definitions and intepretation of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="chp_I__term_1" data-eId="chp_I__term_1">this by-law</span>
</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_1" data-eId="sec_1"><h3>1. Definitions and interpretation</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_1">this by-law</span>, words used in the masculine gender include the feminine, the singular includes the plural and vice versa, and unless the context otherwise indicates</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-above_ground_storage_tank">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-above_ground_storage_tank">above ground storage tank</span>" means a tank situated above ground for the storage of flammable substances as contemplated in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_2">SANS</span> 0131 and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_3">SANS</span> 089 Part 1 and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_4">SANS</span> 087 Part 3;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-agricultural_holding">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-agricultural_holding">agricultural holding</span>" means a portion of land used solely or mainly for the purpose of agriculture, horticulture or for breeding or keeping domesticated animals, poultry or bees;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-approved">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-approved">approved</span>" means as approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_5">municipality</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-automatic_releasing_hold_open_device">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-automatic_releasing_hold_open_device">automatic releasing hold-open device</span>" means a device used to hold open a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_door" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_6">fire door</span> and operates on the detection of a fire to close the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_door" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_7">fire door</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-boundary">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-boundary">boundary</span>" means any lateral or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-street" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_8" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_8">street</span> boundary of a site;</span><span class="akn-blockList" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-building">building</span>" means</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">any structure, whether of a temporary or permanent nature and irrespective of the materials used in the construction thereof, erected or used for or in connection with:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the accommodation or convenience of human beings or animals;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">the manufacture, processing, storage or sale of any goods;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">the rendering of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii__term_1">service</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">the destruction or treatment of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-combustible_refuse" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iv__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iv__term_1">combustible refuse</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-combustible_waste" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iv__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iv__term_2">combustible waste</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks">fireworks</span>" means any explosive device or substance which burns or explodes after ignition, including firecrackers, and which is regulated under the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Explosives_Act" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_38" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_38">Explosives Act</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks_display">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks_display">fireworks display</span>" means the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_39" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_39">use</span> of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_40" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_40">fireworks</span> for purposes of public display;</span><span class="akn-blockList" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_gas" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_6" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_6"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_gas">flammable gas</span>" means a gas which at 20 C and a standard pressure of 101,3 kilopascals</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_6__item_a" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_6__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">is ignitable when in a mixture of 13% or less by volume with air; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_6__item_b" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_6__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">has a flammable range with air of at least 12%, regardless of the lower flammable limit;</span></span></span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_liquid">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_liquid">flammable liquid</span>" means a liquid or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-combustible_liquid" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_41" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_41">combustible liquid</span> which has a closed-cap flash point of 93 C or below;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_solid">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_solid">flammable solid</span>" as contemplated in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_42" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_42">SANS</span> 0228, means a solid that is easily ignited by external sources, such as sparks and flames, solids that are readily combustible, solids that are liable to cause, or contribute to, a fire through friction or solids that are desensitised (wetted) <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-explosives" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_43" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_43">explosives</span> that can explode if not diluted sufficiently;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_store">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_store">flammable store</span>" means a store that is used for the storage of flammable liquids and complies with the criteria set out in Chapter 9 of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_44" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_44">this by-law</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance">flammable substance</span>" means any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_liquid" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_45" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_45">flammable liquid</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-combustible_liquid" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_46" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_46">combustible liquid</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_gas" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_47" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_47">flammable gas</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Group_I__II__III__V__VI__VIII_and_IX_hazardous_substances">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Group_I__II__III__V__VI__VIII_and_IX_hazardous_substances">Group I, II, III, V, VI, VIII and IX hazardous substances</span>" means Group I, II, III, V, VI, VIII and IX hazardous substances, as the case may be, as contemplated in the <span class="akn-term" ambient temperature and pressure and that is maintained in a liquid state by an increase of pressure or lowering of temperature;</span><span class="akn-p" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_b" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">any other functionary or institution</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">exercising a power or performing a function in terms of the <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1996/constitution" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1996/constitution">Constitution</a> or a provincial constitution; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">exercising a public power or performing a public function in terms of any legislation, but does not include a court or judicial officer;</span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-store_room">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-store_room">store room</span>" means a room for storage of flammable substances contemplated in section 79;</span><span class="akn-blockList" data-refersTo="#term-street" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-street">street</span>" means any street, road, cycle path, thoroughfare or any other place, including</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_a" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the verge of any such road, street or thoroughfare;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_b" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">any footpath, sidewalk or similar pedestrian portion of a road reserve;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_c" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">any bridge, ferry or drift traversed by any such road, street or thoroughfare;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">any other object belonging to such road, street or thoroughfare, which has at any time been</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">dedicated to the public;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">used without interruption by the public for a period of at least thirty years;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">declared or rendered such by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_iii__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_iii__term_1">municipality</span> or other competent authority, or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">constructed by a local authority, and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_v" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_v__list_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_v__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">any land, with or without buildings or structures thereon, which is shown as a street on</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_v__list_1__item_aa" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_v__list_1__item_aa"><span class="akn-num">(aa)</span><span class="akn-p">any plan of subdivision or diagram <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approved" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_v__list_1__item_aa__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_v__list_1__item_aa__term_1">approved</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_v__list_1__item_aa__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_v__list_1__item_aa__term_2">municipality</span> or other competent authority and acted upon, or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_v__list_1__item_bb" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_v__list_1__item_bb"><span class="akn-num">(bb)</span><span class="akn-p">any general plan as defined in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Land_Survey_Act" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_v__list_1__item_bb__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_12__item_d__list_1__item_v__list_1__item_bb__term_1">Land Survey Act</span>, 1997 registered or filed in a deeds registry or Surveyor Generals office, unless such land is on such plan                   or diagram described as a private street;</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law">this by-law</span>" includes the Schedules published in terms of this by-law;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-summary_abate">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-summary_abate">summary abate</span>" means to immediately judge a condition to be a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_hazard" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_65" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_65">fire hazard</span> or other threatening danger to life or property and to order immediate correction of such condition;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-underground_tank">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-underground_tank">underground tank</span>" means any tank used or intended to be used for the storage of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_liquid" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_66" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_66">flammable liquid</span> and which is wholly sunk into and below the surface of the ground;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-use">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-use">use</span>" in relation to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_67" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_67">fireworks</span> means discharging, lighting or igniting;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-vegetation">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-vegetation">vegetation</span>" includes grass, weeds, leaves, shrubs and trees; and</span><span class="akn-blockList" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_13" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_13"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle">vehicle</span>" includes a trailer or semi-trailer which</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_13__item_a" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_13__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">has at least 4 wheels with independent axles and suspension systems; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_13__item_b" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_13__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">can be hitched to a truck-tractor or any other motor vehicle contemplated in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-National_Road_Traffic_Act" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_13__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_13__item_b__term_1">National Road Traffic Act</span>.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-West_Coast_District_Municipality">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-West_Coast_District_Municipality">West Coast District Municipality</span>" means the West Coast District <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_68" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_68">municipality</span> established in terms of section 12 of the Municipal Structures <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1998/117" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1998/117">Act, 117 of 1998</a>;</span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_2" data-eId="chp_2"><h2>Chapter 2<br>Purpose and application of by-law</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_2" data-eId="sec_2"><h3>2. Purpose of by-law</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_2__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_2__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The purpose of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_2__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__hcontainer_1__term_1">this by-law</span> is to establish and maintain a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_2__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_2__hcontainer_1__term_2">service</span> for the area of jurisdiction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_2__hcontainer_1__term_3">municipality</span>, to promote the achievement of a fire-safe environment for the benefit of all persons within the area of jurisdiction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__hcontainer_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_2__hcontainer_1__term_4">municipality</span> and to provide for procedures, methods and practices to regulate fire safety within the area of jurisdiction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__hcontainer_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_2__hcontainer_1__term_5">municipality</span>.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_3" data-eId="sec_3"><h3>3. Application of by-law</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_3__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">This by-law is applicable to all persons within the area of jurisdiction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_3__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> and includes both formal and informal sectors of the community and economy.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_3__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding the provisions in either the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Hazardous_Substances_Act" id="sec_3__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__term_1">Hazardous Substances Act</span> or the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Occupational_Health_and_Safety_Act" id="sec_3__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__term_2">Occupational Health and Safety Act</span>, and in addition to any other applicable national or provincial law, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_3__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__term_3">this by-law</span> regulates flammable substances in the area of jurisdiction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_3__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__term_4">municipality</span> so as to prevent and reduce fire hazards or other threatening dangers.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_3__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_3__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_3__term_1">service</span> may, in terms of an agreement as contemplated in section 12 of the Act, and the payment of tariffs in accordance with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_3__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_3__term_2">municipality</span>s tariff policy or as          contemplated in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_3__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_3__term_3">this by-law</span>, be employed outside the area of jurisdiction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_3__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_3__term_4">municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_3__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If any provision in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_3__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4__term_1">this by-law</span> vests or imposes any power, function or duty of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_3__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4__term_2">municipality</span> in or on an employee of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_3__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4__term_3">municipality</span> and such power, function or duty has     in terms of section 81(2) of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipal_Systems_Act" id="sec_3__subsec_4__term_4" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4__term_4">Municipal Systems Act</span> or any other law been assigned to a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_3__subsec_4__term_5" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4__term_5">service</span> provider, the reference in such provision to such employee must be read as     a reference to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_3__subsec_4__term_6" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4__term_6">service</span> provider or, where applicable, an employee of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_3__subsec_4__term_7" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4__term_7">service</span> provider authorized by it.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_3" data-eId="chp_3"><h2>Chapter 3<br>Establishment of a fire brigade <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="chp_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__term_1">service</span>
</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_4" data-eId="sec_4"><h3>4. Establishment and maintenance of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__term_1">service</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_4__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_4__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_1__term_1">service</span> for the area of jurisdiction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_4__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_1__term_2">municipality</span> is established as contemplated in section 3(1) of the Act, read with section 156(1)(a) and Part B of Schedule 4 of     the <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1996/constitution" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1996/constitution">Constitution</a>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_4__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> must maintain the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">service</span>, which includes</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">appointing a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">chief fire officer</span> and the necessary members of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2">service</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">ensuring that such officer and members are properly trained; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">acquiring and maintaining the necessary vehicles, machinery, equipment, devices and accessories to ensure that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">service</span> is effective and able to fulfil its objects.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_5" data-eId="sec_5"><h3>5. Objects of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__term_1">service</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_5__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The objects of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">service</span> are</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">to prevent the outbreak or spread of a fire;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">to fight and extinguish any fire that endangers any person or property;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">to protect any person or property against any fire or other danger as contemplated in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">this by-law</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">to rescue any person or property from any fire or other danger as contemplated in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">this by-law</span>; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">to perform any other function connected with any of the matters referred to in subsection (a) to (d).</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_5__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_5__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_2__term_1">service</span> may provide any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_5__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_2__term_2">service</span> related to its objects to any other person.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_5__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_5__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__term_1">service</span> contemplated in subsection (2) may, at the discretion of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_5__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__term_2">chief fire officer</span>, be terminated without notice if the services, equipment or members involved in       providing that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_5__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__term_3">service</span> are required to deal with an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_5__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__term_4">emergency</span> situation, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_hazard" id="sec_5__subsec_3__term_5" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__term_5">fire hazard</span> or other threatening danger.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_6" data-eId="sec_6"><h3>6. Reporting a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_hazard" id="sec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__term_1">fire hazard</span> and other threatening danger</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_6__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__term_1">owner</span> or the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_6__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__term_2">person in charge</span> of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_6__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__term_3">premises</span>, upon discovering any evidence of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_hazard" id="sec_6__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__term_4">fire hazard</span> or other threatening danger as contemplated in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_6__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__term_5">this by-law</span>, must immediately         notify the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_6__subsec_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__term_6">service</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_6__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_2__term_1">owner</span> or the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_6__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_2__term_2">person in charge</span> of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_6__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_2__term_3">premises</span> must provide all details pertaining to the incident as contemplated in subsection (1), to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_6__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_2__term_4">service</span> as requested.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1) and (2) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_7" data-eId="sec_7"><h3>7. Administration and enforcement</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_7__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span> is responsible for the administration and enforcement of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_7__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1__term_2">this by-law</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where no <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_7__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_2__term_1">chief fire officer</span> has been appointed, or where no acting <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_7__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_2__term_2">chief fire officer</span> has been appointed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_7__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_2__term_3">municipal manager</span> as contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_9" href="#sec_9">section 9</a>(3), the municipal manager is responsible for the administration and enforcement of this by-law.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where there is no <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_7__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__term_1">service</span> established in the area of jurisdiction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__term_2">municipality</span>, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_7__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__term_3">municipal manager</span> is responsible for the administration and enforcement of this by    -law.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_8" data-eId="sec_8"><h3>8. Delegation</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_8__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_8__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span> may delegate any power granted to him in terms of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_8__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1__term_2">this by-law</span> as contemplated in section 19 of the Act or in accordance with the system of delegation      of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_8__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1__term_3">municipality</span> developed in terms of section 59 of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipal_Systems_Act" id="sec_8__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1__term_4">Municipal Systems Act</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_8__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_8__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2__term_1">municipal manager</span> may delegate any power granted to him in terms of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_8__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2__term_2">this by-law</span> in accordance with the system of delegation of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_8__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2__term_3">municipality</span> developed in terms of           section 59 of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipal_Systems_Act" id="sec_8__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2__term_4">Municipal Systems Act</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_9" data-eId="sec_9"><h3>9. Chief fire officer</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span> has the powers as contemplated in sections 8(1) and 8(2) of the Act, and must also</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">make or implement such general orders, procedures, rules and such other measures as he may consider necessary for the proper administration and enforcement of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">this by-law</span>; provided that the making or implementation of such general orders, procedures, rules and such other measures are not inconsistent with the provisions of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">this by-law</span> or any other by-law or policy of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_3">municipality</span>.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">ensure that contact numbers in respect of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">service</span> are made available to the public and other institutions or organisations;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">inform the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">municipal manager</span> of operational requirements for the structuring of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2">service</span> as contemplated in section 5.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding anything to the contrary contained in any other law, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_9__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_2__term_1">chief fire officer</span> has the authority to investigate the cause, origin and circumstances of any fire or other threatening danger.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Whenever the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_9__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_3__term_1">chief fire officer</span> is for any reason unable to perform his duties of office, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_9__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_3__term_2">municipal manager</span> must appoint a suitably qualified <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_9__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_3__term_3">member</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_9__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_3__term_4">service</span> as acting <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_9__subsec_3__term_5" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_3__term_5">chief fire officer</span> to perform the duties and functions of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_9__subsec_3__term_6" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_3__term_6">chief fire officer</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_10" data-eId="sec_10"><h3>10. Instructions by members of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_10__term_1" data-eId="sec_10__term_1">service</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_10__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In addition to any powers as contemplated in section 8 of the Act, a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_10__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_1__term_1">member</span> may give any instruction to any person in order to secure compliance with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_10__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_1__term_2">this by-law</span> or to ensure     the safety of any person or property.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_10__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An instruction may be given orally or in writing and if the instruction is given orally, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_10__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_2__term_1">member</span> must confirm it in writing and give it to the person concerned at the         earliest opportunity.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_10__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An instruction contemplated in subsection (1) may include, but is not limited to an instruction</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">for the immediate evacuation of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">premises</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">to close or barricade any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">premises</span>, or part thereof, until such time as any contravention of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2">this by-law</span> has been rectified;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">to cease any activity;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">to remove any immediate threat to the safety of any person or property;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">to take specified steps to comply with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__term_1">this by-law</span>, either immediately or within a specified period; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">if it is not reasonable for steps referred to in paragraph (e) to be taken immediately for the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_f__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_f__term_2" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_f__term_2">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_f__term_3" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_f__term_3">premises</span> concerned, to provide the chief          fire officer with a written description of the steps to be taken and a time-table for the taking of these steps in order to ensure compliance with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_f__term_4" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__list_1__item_f__term_4">this by-law</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_10__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (3) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_11" data-eId="sec_11"><h3>11. Powers of members of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_11__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__term_1">service</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_11__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">member</span> of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">service</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">municipality</span> may, whenever he regards it necessary or expedient in order to perform his functions, perform any act, and may also </span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">close any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-street" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">street</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">enter or break and enter any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">premises</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">damage, destroy or pull down any property</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">forcibly remove or cause to be removed from the scene any person who is in danger or who obstructs that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1">member</span> in the performance of his duties; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">take material or any object from any person: Provided that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_1">owner</span> of the material or object so taken be compensated therefor by the controlling authority concerned to an amount agreed upon by the controlling authority and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_2">owner</span>, or in the absence of such agreement, an amount determined by arbitration in accordance with the provisions of the Arbitration Act, 1965 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1965/42" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1965/42">Act 42 of 1965</a>).</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_11__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_11__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_3__term_1">member</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_11__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_3__term_2">service</span> of a controlling authority, including a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_11__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_3__term_3">chief fire officer</span>, may, whenever he regards it necessary in order to perform his functions, order any inhabitant of the republic who is not younger than 16 years and not older than 60 years to assist him in the performance of his functions on any particular occasion.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_12" data-eId="sec_12"><h3>12. Fire brigade reserve force</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_12__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_12__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> may establish a fire brigade reserve force for its area of jurisdiction.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_12__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_12__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_2__term_1">chief fire officer</span> may, on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed" id="sec_12__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_2__term_2">prescribed</span> conditions, appoint a person who applies therefor, as a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_12__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_2__term_3">member</span> of the fire brigade reserve force.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_12__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_12__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_3__term_1">member</span> of a fire brigade reserve force shall be a temporary <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_12__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_3__term_2">member</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_12__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_3__term_3">service</span> and shall perform the functions entrusted to him by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_12__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_3__term_4">chief fire officer</span>, or a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_12__subsec_3__term_5" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_3__term_5">member</span> of     the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_12__subsec_3__term_6" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_3__term_6">service</span> acting on behalf of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_12__subsec_3__term_7" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_3__term_7">chief fire officer</span>: Provided that a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_12__subsec_3__term_8" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_3__term_8">member</span> of a fire brigade reserve force may, as far as possible, only be employed for the performance      of those functions for which he, in the opinion of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_12__subsec_3__term_9" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_3__term_9">chief fire officer</span>, has received adequate training.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_12__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_12__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_4__term_1">chief fire officer</span> may at any time discharge a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_12__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_4__term_2">member</span> of the fire brigade reserve force.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_12__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_12__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_5__term_1">member</span> of the fire brigade reserve force shall have the same powers as a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_12__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_5__term_2">member</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_12__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_5__term_3">service</span> and shall, in the performance of his functions, be regarded as a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_12__subsec_5__term_4" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_5__term_4">member</span> of       <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_12__subsec_5__term_5" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_5__term_5">service</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_13" data-eId="sec_13"><h3>13. Pretending to be <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_13__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__term_1">member</span> of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_13__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__term_2">service</span> prohibited</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may pretend to be a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_13__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1__term_1">member</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person who is not a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_13__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_2__term_1">member</span> may wear any official clothing, uniform, badge or insignia of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_13__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_2__term_2">service</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1) and (2) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_14" data-eId="sec_14"><h3>14. Certificates to identify members of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_14__term_1" data-eId="sec_14__term_1">service</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_14__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_14__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span> must provide each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_14__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_1__term_2">member</span> with an identification document identifying that person as a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_14__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_1__term_3">member</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_14__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">member</span>, while performing any function or exercising any power as contemplated in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">this by-law</span> must</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">keep the identification document provided in terms of subsection (1), on his person; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">produce it for inspection on request by any person.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_15" data-eId="sec_15"><h3>15. Wearing of uniform and insignia</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_15__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_15__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span> and every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_15__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__term_2">member</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_15__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__term_3">service</span> must wear the uniform, rank markings and insignia of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_15__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__term_4">service</span> as <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed" id="sec_15__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__term_5">prescribed</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_15__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Uniform, rank markings and insignia as contemplated in subsection (1) must be issued to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_15__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__term_1">chief fire officer</span> and members of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_15__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__term_2">service</span> in accordance with the conditions of     employment of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_15__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__term_3">municipality</span> or as agreed collectively.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_16" data-eId="sec_16"><h3>16. Driving <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_16__term_1" data-eId="sec_16__term_1">service</span> vehicles</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_16__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_16__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_1__term_1">member</span> may, with the written authority of the Chief Fire Officer and as directed in the exercise of his or her duties, drive a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_16__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_1__term_2">service</span> <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_16__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_1__term_3">vehicle</span> if he or she is in possession     of a valid driving licence for the code of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_16__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_1__term_4">vehicle</span> in question.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_16__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_16__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_2__term_1">member</span>, who is duly authorised to do so, as contemplated in subsection (1), must drive a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_16__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_2__term_2">service</span> <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_16__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_2__term_3">vehicle</span> in accordance with the provisions of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-National_Road_Traffic_Act" id="sec_16__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_2__term_4">National Road Traffic Act</span>,     1996, and any regulations made under the Act.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_16__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_16__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_3__term_1">member</span> who fails to comply with the provisions of this section is guilty of an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_17" data-eId="sec_17"><h3>17. Duties and orders during <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_17__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__term_1">emergency</span> situations</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_17__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The Chief Fire Officer or a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">member</span> in charge of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">emergency</span> situation, including one attended in terms of an agreement, must, in respect of every such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">emergency</span> situation,      ensure that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">adequate manpower and the appropriate apparatus and equipment are made available, deployed and are used without delay;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">emergency</span> situation is immediately assessed upon arrival and additional resources or assistance that he/she may deem necessary, are called for without delay.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">all pertinent information, including information about places and times and relevant particulars, is recorded during the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">emergency</span> situation or as soon as possible after         the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2">emergency</span> situation, and that the recorded information is preserved in accordance with the provisions of the National Archives of South Africa Act, 1996 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1996/43" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1996/43">Act 43 of          1996</a>), and any regulations made under the Act.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_17__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person or body, including any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-State" id="sec_17__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_2__term_1">State</span> department as contemplated in section 17 of the Act, the South African Police Service and the Department of Justice, who wishes to        inspect any information referred to in subsection (1)(c) must send a motivated request in writing to the Chief Fire Officer along with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed" id="sec_17__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_2__term_2">prescribed</span> fees.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_17__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any press or media release concerning the Service, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_17__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_3__term_1">emergency</span> situations or any matter in relation thereto must be in accordance with the policy guidelines determined by the      <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_17__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_3__term_2">municipality</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_18" data-eId="sec_18"><h3>18. Right of access to buildings and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_18__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__term_1">premises</span> and issue of instructions</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Chief Fire Officer or a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_18__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_1__term_1">member</span> may, in executing the powers delegated in terms of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_18__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_1__term_2">this by-law</span> or any other legislation, enter any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_18__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_1__term_3">premises</span> at any reasonable time to          conduct inspections in order to determine the existence of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_hazard" id="sec_18__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_1__term_4">fire hazard</span> or compliance with any applicable legislation relating to fire safety on such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_18__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_1__term_5">premises</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Should any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_hazard" id="sec_18__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2__term_1">fire hazard</span> or condition of non-compliance contemplated in subsection (1) exist, such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_18__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2__term_2">member</span> may serve a written instruction on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_18__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2__term_3">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupier" id="sec_18__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2__term_4">occupier</span> of such          <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_18__subsec_2__term_5" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2__term_5">premises</span> and such notice shall incorporate such directives and/ or requirements that are necessary to abate the condition, which instruction must determine a deadline for        compliance.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Whenever any condition that may increase the risk of fire or which may pose a threat to life or property exists on any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_18__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_3__term_1">premises</span> and such condition cannot be immediately          rectified, or if costs need to be incurred to rectify such condition, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_18__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_3__term_2">owner</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_18__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_3__term_3">premises</span> must, after receiving any written instruction referred to in subsection (2),      inform the Chief Fire Officer forthwith, in writing, of the measures which he or she intends taking to remedy the condition and provide a programme and deadline to the Chief     Fire Officer for approval.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Chief Fire Officer may approve the proposed measures and deadline with or without amendments and may give further instructions for compliance with the proposed or            required measures.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who fails to comply with a written instruction referred to in this section is guilty of an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_19" data-eId="sec_19"><h3>19. Interference with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_19__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__term_1">service</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may interfere with, prevent, obstruct or hinder the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_19__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_19__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__term_2">municipal manager</span> or any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_19__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__term_3">member</span> in the execution of his duties as contemplated in this by       -law or the Act.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_20" data-eId="sec_20"><h3>20. Furnishing of false information</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may wilfully give any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_20__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__term_1">member</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_20__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__term_2">service</span> any notice, or furnish any information regarding an outbreak of fire, or any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_20__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__term_3">emergency</span> situation requiring the        attendance of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_20__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__term_4">service</span>, which is false or inaccurate.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_21" data-eId="sec_21"><h3>21. Denial, suspension or revocation of an approval or a certificate</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_21__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span> may refuse, suspend or revoke an approval or a certificate required by <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">this by-law</span> for</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">failure to meet the provisions of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">this by-law</span> for the issuance of the approval or certificate; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">non-compliance with the provisions of the approval or certificate.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_22" data-eId="sec_22"><h3>22. Records required, access to records and release of media statements</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_22__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The safekeeping of all relevant records and documents pertaining to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_22__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_1__term_1">service</span> in accordance with the provisions of the National Archives and Record Service of South Africa     Act is the responsibility of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_22__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_1__term_2">municipal manager</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_22__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A request for access to a record held for the purpose or with regard to the exercise of a power or the performance of a function in respect of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_22__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_2__term_1">service</span> must be made in        accordance with the provisions of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Promotion_of_Access_to_Information_Act" id="sec_22__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_2__term_2">Promotion of Access to
