Information Act</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_22__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Media statements regarding the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_22__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__term_1">service</span> must be released as <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed" id="sec_22__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__term_2">prescribed</span> in terms of the communication strategy of the Municipality.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_23" data-eId="sec_23"><h3>23. Failure to comply with provisions</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">When the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span> finds that there is non-compliance with the provisions of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">this by-law</span>, excluding the situation in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_16" href="#sec_16">section 16</a>(2), a written notice      must be issued and include the following</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">confirmation of the findings;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">provisions of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">this by-law</span> that are being contravened;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the remedial action required; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">a time for compliance.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An order or notice issued under <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_23__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__term_1">this by-law</span> must be served either by personal delivery or registered mail upon a person who is in the opinion of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_23__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__term_2">chief fire officer</span>,          deemed to be the appropriate person.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">For unattended or abandoned <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_23__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3__term_1">premises</span>, a copy of such order or notice must be posted on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_23__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3__term_2">premises</span> in a conspicuous place at or near the entrance to such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_23__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3__term_3">premises</span> and the       order or notice must be mailed by registered mail, to the last known address of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_23__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3__term_4">owner</span>, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_23__subsec_3__term_5" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3__term_5">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_23__subsec_3__term_6" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3__term_6">premises</span> or both.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_23__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_4__term_1">owner</span> or the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_23__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_4__term_2">person in charge</span> of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_23__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_4__term_3">premises</span>, whose rights are affected by any decision of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_23__subsec_4__term_4" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_4__term_4">chief fire officer</span> as contemplated in subsection (1), may appeal against such      decision in terms of section 62 of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipal_Systems_Act" id="sec_23__subsec_4__term_5" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_4__term_5">Municipal Systems Act</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_24" data-eId="sec_24"><h3>24. Payment for services</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_24__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_24__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> may charge the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed" id="sec_24__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__term_2">prescribed</span> tariff payable by a person on whose behalf the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_24__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__term_3">municipality</span> rendered any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_24__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__term_4">service</span> as contemplated in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_24__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__term_5">this by-law</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_24__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_24__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span> may charge a tariff for the provision of an inspection, re-inspection or any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_24__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_2__term_2">service</span>, including the approval or issuing of permits or certificates as      contemplated in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_24__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_2__term_3">this by-law</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_24__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any cost incurred by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_24__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__term_1">municipality</span> for any action necessary to prevent a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_hazard" id="sec_24__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__term_2">fire hazard</span>, accident or other threatening danger shall be considered a tariff payable by a person     for services rendered as contemplated in subsection (1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_24__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any costs incurred by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_24__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_4__term_1">municipality</span> in connection with the examination or analysis of any sample taken from any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_24__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_4__term_2">premises</span> for the purposes of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_24__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_4__term_3">this by-law</span>, and a report on      such analysis by an institution accredited by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_24__subsec_4__term_4" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_4__term_4">chief fire officer</span> for that purpose may be recovered from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_24__subsec_4__term_5" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_4__term_5">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_24__subsec_4__term_6" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_4__term_6">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_24__subsec_4__term_7" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_4__term_7">premises</span> if such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_24__subsec_4__term_8" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_4__term_8">owner</span> or        <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_24__subsec_4__term_9" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_4__term_9">person in charge</span> is not in compliance with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_24__subsec_4__term_10" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_4__term_10">this by-law</span> regarding the substance concerned.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_25" data-eId="sec_25"><h3>25. Joint Fire Services Committee</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_25__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A Joint Fire Services Committee representing the fire services in the area of jurisdiction of the West Coast District <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_25__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> and all Category B Municipalities in the       area of jurisdiction of such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_25__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_1__term_2">municipality</span> may be established.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_25__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The Joint Fire Services Committee as contemplated in subsection (1) must collaborate and liaise for the purposes of making recommendations with regard to</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the planning and co-ordination of the services within the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-district" id="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">district</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the co-ordination and standardisation of infrastructure, vehicles, equipment and procedures pertaining to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">service</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the training of members; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">any other operational matters relating to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1">service</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_25__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_25__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_3__term_1">chief fire officer</span> of each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_25__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_3__term_2">municipality</span> within the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-district" id="sec_25__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_3__term_3">district</span> may be a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_25__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_3__term_4">member</span> of the Joint Fire Services Committee.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_25__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Joint Fire Services Committee may determine its rules of meeting procedures, provided that such procedures are not inconsistent with generally accepted municipal             administrative practices, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_25__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_4__term_1">this by-law</span> or any other legislation.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_4" data-eId="chp_4"><h2>Chapter 4<br>Fire protection</h2>
<section class="akn-part" id="chp_4__part_A" data-eId="chp_4__part_A"><h2>Part A  Fire protection for buildings and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="chp_4__part_A__term_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_A__term_1">premises</span>
</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_26" data-eId="sec_26"><h3>26. General provisions</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span> must in terms of sections <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_16" href="#sec_16">16</a>(3) and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_21" href="#sec_21">21</a>(1) of this by-law abate a contravention of the National Building Regulations relating to fire and safety of buildings and premises.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_27" data-eId="sec_27"><h3>27. Design and construction of buildings</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_27__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Subject to the provisions of subsection (3), every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">owner</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">building</span>, excluding a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dwelling_house" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">dwelling house</span>, must ensure that it is designed and constructed in a manner that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">provides for</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the effective drainage of any water that may result from fire extinguishing activities; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">the discharge of such water directly into a storm water drain;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">prevents any water that may result from fire-extinguishing activities from draining</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">down any stairway or lift shaft;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">down any electrical shaft or telecommunications <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1">service</span> shaft;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">down any shaft that is connected to a basement level; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">along any approach to a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iv__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iv__term_1">building</span> or any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iv__term_2" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iv__term_2">vehicle</span> access ramp leading to or from a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iv__term_3" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iv__term_3">building</span>;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">if any water resulting from fire-extinguishing activities should spill into a basement, such water is discharged directly into a storm water drain; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">complies with the requirements of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">SANS</span> 0400 (Parts A, K, M, O, T, V and W) insofar as it relates to fire protection.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_27__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_27__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Subject to the provisions of subsection (3), every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_27__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">owner</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_27__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">building</span> equipped with a transformer room must ensure that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the transformer room is situated on the ground level;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">access to the transformer room is from outside the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_27__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">building</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">there is adequate and ready access to the transformer room for fire-fighting and maintenance activities.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_27__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Subsections (1) and (2) do not apply in respect of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_27__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_3__term_1">building</span> which exists at the commencement of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_27__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_3__term_2">this by-law</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_27__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1) and (2) or Parts A, K, M, O, T, V or W of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_27__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__subsec_4__term_1">SANS</span> 10400 in so far as it relates to fire protection, commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_28" data-eId="sec_28"><h3>28. Access for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_28__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__term_1">emergency</span> vehicles</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_28__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">When, in the opinion of the controlling authority, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">premises</span> are not readily accessible from public roads it must be provided with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">emergency</span> <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">vehicle</span> access and, notwithstandin     g the provisions in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-National_Building_Regulations" id="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__term_4">National Building Regulations</span> (T1) , may be required to comply with the following:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">An access road must be constructed so that it is capable of supporting the mass of the heaviest <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">emergency</span> <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">vehicle</span> required to cater for the risk of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_3">premises</span>.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">A motorized or electronically operated gate must be equipped in such a manner that access to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">premises</span> can be gained without the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">use</span> of a motor or any other electronic         device.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">Fire lanes must be provided for all <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">premises</span> which are set back more than 45 meters from a public road or exceed nine meters in height and are set back over 15 meters            from a public road.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">Fire lanes must be at least four meters in width, the position of which must be decided upon after consultation with the controlling authority, and the area from ground          level to a clearance height of four meters above the fire lane must remain unobstructed.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">A cul-de-sac that is more than 90 meters in length, must be provided with a minimum turning circle at the closed end of the road capable of accommodating the largest             <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1">emergency</span> <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_2" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_2">vehicle</span> which is required to cater for the risk of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_3" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_3">premises</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_28__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The design, marking, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_28__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_2__term_1">use</span> and maintenance of fire lanes not forming part of a public road must comply with the requirements of the controlling authority.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_28__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">It is unlawful for a person to park a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_28__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__term_1">vehicle</span> in or otherwise obstruct a fire lane.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_28__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span
