manner that it causes an obstruction to a fire hydrant.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_29" data-eId="sec_29"><h3>29. Design and construction of dumping sites</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every person who designs or constructs any dumping site, must ensure that it is designed and constructed in accordance with the instructions of</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the Department of Environmental Affairs; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">municipality</span>.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_30" data-eId="sec_30"><h3>30. Design and construction of other structures and sites</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_30__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every person who designs, constructs or erects any of the following structures, must ensure that they comply with a rational design as contemplated by the National Building      Regulations</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">any grain silo;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">any atrium;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">any air traffic control tower;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">any tower for telecommunications or other uses;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">any thatched structure which is larger than 20 square metres and situated within 4.5 metres of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-boundary" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1">boundary</span> line of the property concerned;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">any tent or other temporary structure for holding a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_gathering" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_1">public gathering</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">any open-plan commercial or industrial <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_1">premises</span> with a covering distance that exceeds 45 metres measured from any point in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_2" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_2">premises</span> to any escape or exit door.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_30__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every person who designs or constructs any aircraft hanger or helicopter pad, must ensure that it</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">complies with a rational design as contemplated by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-National_Building_Regulations" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">National Building Regulations</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">provides for the effective drainage of any liquid from the floor of the hanger or helicopter pad or any approach to the aircraft hanger or helicopter pad;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">provides for the effective channelling of any liquid from the floor of the hanger or helicopter pad to a drainage area connected to a separator well;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">prevents the spread of any liquid from the floor of the hanger or helicopter pad; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">is equipped with effective earthing devices for the discharge of static electricity.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_30__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1) and (2) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_31" data-eId="sec_31"><h3>31. Requirements for sprinkler systems</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_31__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If a sprinkler system is required in any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_31__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1__term_1">building</span> in accordance with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_31__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1__term_2">SANS</span> 0400, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_31__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1__term_3">SANS</span> 087 (Part III) or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_31__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1__term_4">SANS</span> 089 (Part I) or if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_31__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1__term_5">chief fire officer</span> so requires, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_31__subsec_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1__term_6">owner</span>      or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_31__subsec_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1__term_7">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_31__subsec_1__term_8" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1__term_8">premises</span> must ensure that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_31__subsec_1__term_9" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1__term_9">building</span> is equipped with a sprinkler system.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_31__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every person who designs, constructs or installs a sprinkler system must ensure that it is designed, constructed and installed</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">in accordance with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">SANS</span> 0287; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">in compliance with the requirements of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">SANS</span> 0400 (Parts A, K, M, O, T, V and W) insofar as it relates to fire protection.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_31__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1) and (2) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_32" data-eId="sec_32"><h3>32. Requirements for extractor fan systems</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_32__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every person who designs, constructs or installs an extractor fan system, any related ducts or any similar chimney system and every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">building</span>     in which such a system is installed must ensure that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">it is designed, constructed and installed in a manner that provides for clearly demarcated, adequate and easy access for inspection, maintenance and repairs; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the conduit and outlet of any such system is installed in a manner that does not result in a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_hazard" id="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">fire hazard</span> to any person or property.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_32__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_32__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_2__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_32__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_2__term_2">person in charge</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_32__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_2__term_3">building</span> in which an extractor fan system, any related ducts or any similar chimney system has been installed, must ensure that every        filter, damper, screen or conduit forming an integral part of the system is regularly inspected, cleaned and maintained to ensure that fatty residues or any other combustible     residues do not accumulate.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_32__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_32__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1) and (2) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_33" data-eId="sec_33"><h3>33. Requirements for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_33__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__term_1">emergency</span> exits</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">owner</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">building</span> must ensure that any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-escape_door" id="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">escape door</span> in that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__term_4">building</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">is fitted with hinges that open in the direction of escape; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">is equipped with a fail-safe locking device or devices that do not require a key in order to exit.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">owner</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">building</span> must ensure that any door in a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-feeder_route" id="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1__term_3">feeder route</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">is a double swing-type door;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">is not equipped with any locking mechanism.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding the provisions of subsection (2), if it is necessary that a door in a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-feeder_route" id="sec_33__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__term_1">feeder route</span> be locked for security reasons, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_33__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__term_2">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_33__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__term_3">person in charge</span> of the           <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_33__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__term_4">building</span> must provide an alternative means of escape <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approved" id="sec_33__subsec_3__term_5" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__term_5">approved</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_33__subsec_3__term_6" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__term_6">chief fire officer</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may obstruct or allow the obstruction of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-escape_route" id="sec_33__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__term_1">escape route</span> from any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_33__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__term_2">premises</span> that may prevent or hinder the escape of any person or animal from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_33__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__term_3">premises</span> in an       <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_33__subsec_4__term_4" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_4__term_4">emergency</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where required by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_33__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_5__term_1">chief fire officer</span>, an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-escape_route" id="sec_33__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_5__term_2">escape route</span> must be clearly indicated with signage, which complies with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_33__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_5__term_3">SANS</span> 1186, indicating the direction of travel in the        event of fire or any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_33__subsec_5__term_4" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_5__term_4">emergency</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1), (2), (3), (4) and (5) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_34" data-eId="sec_34"><h3>34. Requirement regarding fire doors and assemblies</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_34__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Subject to the provisions of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_34__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_1__term_1">SANS</span> 1253, a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_door" id="sec_34__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_1__term_2">fire door</span> and assembly must be maintained in such a manner that in the event of a fire it retains its integrity, insulation and         stability for the time period required for that particular <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-class" id="sec_34__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_1__term_3">class</span> of door.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_34__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_door" id="sec_34__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2__term_1">fire door</span> may be kept open, only when it is equipped with an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-automatic_releasing_hold_open_device" id="sec_34__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2__term_2">automatic releasing hold-open device</span> <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approved" id="sec_34__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2__term_3">approved</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_34__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2__term_4">chief fire officer</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_34__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_34__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_door" id="sec_34__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">fire door</span> and assembly may not be rendered less effective through the following actions</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_34__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">altering the integrity, insulation or stability of a particular <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-class" id="sec_34__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">class</span> of door;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_34__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">disconnecting the self-closing mechanism;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_34__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">wedging, blocking or obstructing the door so that it cannot close;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_34__subsec_3__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_3__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">painting the fusible link actuating mechanism of a door;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_34__subsec_3__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_3__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">disconnecting or rendering less effective an electric or electronic release mechanism, or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_34__subsec_3__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_3__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">any other action that renders a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_door" id="sec_34__subsec_3__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_3__list_1__item_f__term_1">fire door</span> or assembly less effective.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_34__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1), (2) and (3) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_35" data-eId="sec_35"><h3>35. Design, identification and access for fire-fighting and rescue purposes</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_35__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Subject to the requirements of any applicable zoning scheme regulations or the conditions of establishment of any township, every person who plans, designs or constructs a       <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">building</span>, excluding a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dwelling_house" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">dwelling house</span>, must ensure that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">premises</span> on which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__term_4">building</span> is situated, are planned, designed and constructed so that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">at least one elevation of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">building</span> fronts onto a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-street" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">street</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">premises</span> do not front onto a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-street" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">street</span>, an access road is provided with dimensions and carrying capacity <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approved" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_3">approved</span> in writing by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_4" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_4">chief fire officer</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">a motorised or electronically operated gate is equipped in such a manner that access to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">premises</span> can be gained without the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2">use</span> of a motor or any other electronic             device or any other assistance;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__list_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">there is a climate-proof and weather-proof parking surface for parking and operating fire brigade machines and equipment in an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__term_1">emergency</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">of dimensions at least 10 metres wide;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">that runs the full length of the side elevation of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ii__term_1">building</span> that borders the surface; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">with a carrying capacity of at least 70 metric tons; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">any entrance arch to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iv__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iv__term_1">premises</span> provides an opening with dimensions at least 4 metres wide  4.2 metres high, unless there is an alternative and easy access route              to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iv__term_2" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iv__term_2">premises</span> of at least the same dimensions.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_35__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">For purposes of easy identification by any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">member</span> in an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">emergency</span>, every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_3">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_4">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_5">premises</span> must ensure that the correct <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-street" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_6">street</span> number of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_7">premises</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">is displayed clearly on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-street" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">street</span> <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-boundary" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2">boundary</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_3">premises</span> in numbers at least 75 millimetres high;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">is visible from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-street" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">street</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">is maintained in a legible condition at all times.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_35__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1) and (2) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_36" data-eId="sec_36"><h3>36. Accessibility of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_fighting_equipment" id="sec_36__term_1" data-eId="sec_36__term_1">fire-fighting equipment</span> and fire installations</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_36__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_fighting_equipment" id="sec_36__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_1__term_1">fire-fighting equipment</span> or fire protection installations installed on any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_36__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_1__term_2">premises</span> must be accessible to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_36__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_1__term_3">service</span> at all times.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_36__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person, who causes or permits any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_fighting_equipment" id="sec_36__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_36__subsec_2__term_1">fire-fighting equipment</span> or fire protection installations to be obstructed or impedes such accessibility or operation, commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_37" data-eId="sec_37"><h3>37. Barricading of vacant buildings</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_37__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">person in charge</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">building</span> or portion of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__term_4">building</span> that is vacant must, to the satisfaction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__term_5">chief fire officer</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">remove all <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-combustible_waste" id="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">combustible waste</span> and refuse from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">building</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">block, barricade or otherwise secure all windows, doors and other openings in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">building</span> in a manner that will prevent the creation of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_hazard" id="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">fire hazard</span> caused by                entering of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_3">building</span> by any unauthorised person.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_37__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_37__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_38" data-eId="sec_38"><h3>38. Division and occupancy separating elements</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_38__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_38__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_38__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__hcontainer_1__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_38__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_38__hcontainer_1__term_2">person in charge</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_38__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_38__hcontainer_1__term_3">building</span> may not alter a division or occupancy separating element in any way that would render it less effective or to allow flame, heat or combustion products from penetrating into the adjacent compartment or structure.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_39" data-eId="sec_39"><h3>39. Tents</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_39__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_39__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Prior to the erection and usage of a tent as an occupancy contemplated in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-National_Building_Regulations" id="sec_39__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">National Building Regulations</span> (A20), an applicant must:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_39__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">submit an application in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-National_Building_Regulations" id="sec_39__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">National Building Regulations</span> (A2) to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_39__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">municipality</span> for the erection and usage of the tent, and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_39__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">submit an application in terms of the section 56 of this By-law to the controlling authority for a temporary population certificate.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_39__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The application submitted in terms of subsection (1)(a) must comply with the following:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">The tent must be erected at least 4,5 meters from a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-boundary" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">boundary</span>, combustible store or material and the controlling authority may require that this distance be increased             should the situation require it.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">Where tents are erected adjacent to one another, an unobstructed minimum distance of 4,5 meters must be provided between them and where applicable between the stakes and         guidelines of the adjacent tents, in order to ensure <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">emergency</span> <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2">vehicle</span> access.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The requirements set out in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-National_Building_Regulations" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__term_1">National Building Regulations</span> (T1) must be complied with in the following instances:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">where the population of a tent exceeds 25 people;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">where a tent is occupied during the hours of darkness;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">for seating arrangements and aisle dimensions, and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">for the provisions of fire extinguishers.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">The population density of a tent must comply with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-National_Building_Regulations" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1">National Building Regulations</span> (A21).</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">No cooking may be carried out in the tent occupied by the public and where cooking is required, it must be carried out in a separate tent or an area to which the public          does not have access.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">No open fire is permitted in a tent and any other flame emitting device, such as a candle, lantern or torch but not limited thereto, is only permitted in a tent after            approval by the controlling authority.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">No open fire or flame is permitted within five meters of a tent, stake or guideline of a tent.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">Smoking is prohibited in a tent and a "No Smoking" sign must be prominently displayed at each entrance and must comply with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_h__term_1" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_h__term_1">SANS</span> 1186-1.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">Lighting and wiring installed in a tent must comply with the requirements set out in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_i__term_1">SANS</span> 10142 in such a manner that direct contact is not made with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-combustible_material" id="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_i__term_2" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_2__list_1__item_i__term_2">combustible material</span>         and the radiated heat does not pose an ignition hazard.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_39__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_39__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding the provisions in subsections (1) and (2), the controlling authority may request the applicant to fulfil additional requirements for the erection and usage of     a tent.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_40" data-eId="sec_40"><h3>40. Informal settlements</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_40__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_40__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_40__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_40__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">In the event of establishment of any informal settlement, inclusive of any temporary settlement area, the following minimum requirements shall apply:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_40__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a safety distance of 3 metres between structures shall be maintained;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_40__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the settlement must be divided into blocks of not more than 20 structures per block, with a minimum distance of 6 metres between blocks.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_40__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">Access roads for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_40__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_40__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">emergency</span> vehicles must be at least six meters in width. The position of which must be decided upon after consultation with the controlling authority,           and the area from ground level to a clearance height of five meters above the road must remain unobstructed.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_40__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">A cul-de-sac that is more than 90 meters in length, must be provided with a minimum turning circle at the closed end of the road, capable of accommodating the largest            <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_40__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_40__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">emergency</span> <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_40__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_40__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_2">vehicle</span> which is required to cater for the risk of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_40__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_3" data-eId="sec_40__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_3">premises</span>.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_40__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">Water supply for fire-fighting purposes must be supplied in accordance with Part F (Water Supply for Fire-fighting Purposes) of this bylaw.</span></span></span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_4__part_B" data-eId="chp_4__part_B"><h2>Part B  Fire-fighting equipment</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_41" data-eId="sec_41"><h3>41. Installation and maintenance of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_fighting_equipment" id="sec_41__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__term_1">fire-fighting equipment</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_41__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">owner</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">building</span> must ensure that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">all <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_fighting_equipment" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">fire-fighting equipment</span> and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">service</span> installations on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_3">premises</span> are installed in a manner and condition ready for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_4" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_4">use</span> in an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_5" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_5">emergency</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">all portable and mobile fire-extinguishers and all hose reels on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">premises</span> are serviced and maintained in accordance with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">SANS</span> 0105 and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_3">SANS</span> 1475; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">all <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_fighting_equipment" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__term_1">fire-fighting equipment</span> and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__term_2">service</span> installations on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__term_3">premises</span> are</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">maintained in a good working condition by a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-competent_person" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__term_1">competent person</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">inspected and serviced in accordance with manufacturer specifications; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">are inspected by an appropriately registered and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-competent_person" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii__term_1" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">a comprehensive <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">service</span> record of all <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_fighting_equipment" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_2">fire-fighting equipment</span> and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_3" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_3">service</span> installations on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_4" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_4">premises</span> is maintained and furnished to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_5" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_5">chief fire officer</span> every 12            months or as otherwise directed.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_41__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every person who inspects, services or repairs any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_fighting_equipment" id="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">fire-fighting equipment</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service_installation" id="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">service installation</span> must</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">on completing the inspection, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__term_1">service</span> or repairs, as the case may be</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">certify in writing that the equipment or installation concerned is fully functional; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">furnish that certificate to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_1">owner</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_2" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_2">premises</span>; or</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if the equipment or installation cannot readily be repaired to a functional state, notify the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">chief fire officer</span> of this fact in writing without delay.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_41__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Except for purposes of inspection, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_41__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_3__term_1">service</span>, repair or fire-fighting, no person may remove or interfere with any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_fighting_equipment" id="sec_41__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_3__term_2">fire-fighting equipment</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may alter, damage, misuse or render ineffective any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_fighting_equipment" id="sec_41__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_4__term_1">fire-fighting equipment</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service_installation" id="sec_41__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_41__subsec_4__term_2">service installation</span> at any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1), (2), (3) and (4) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_42" data-eId="sec_42"><h3>42. Fire alarms and fire hydrants</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_42__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Without compensation to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">owner</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">premises</span> concerned, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">chief fire officer</span> may cause:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a fire alarm;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a transmission instrument for calls of fire or other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">emergency</span>, or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">a transmission instrument for warning residents of a fire or other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">emergency</span>, to be affixed to any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2">building</span>, wall, fence, pole or tree.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_42__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Without compensation to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_42__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_2__term_1">owner</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_42__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_2__term_2">premises</span> concerned, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_42__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_2__term_3">chief fire officer</span> may cause the position of a fire hydrant and fire alarm or any other fire protection          information to be marked on any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_42__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_2__term_4">building</span>, wall, fence, pole, tree, road, pavement or hydrant cover with a board, metal plate or painted marker or by any other means, as          <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed" id="sec_42__subsec_2__term_5" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_2__term_5">prescribed</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_42__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_42__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_3__term_1">chief fire officer</span> may at any time cause a fire alarm, other transmission instrument mentioned in subsection (1), board, metal plate or painted marker to be removed          without compensating an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_42__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_3__term_2">owner</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_42__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_3__term_3">premises</span> concerned.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_42__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An unauthorised person is prohibited from removing, defacing, altering, tampering or damaging a fire alarm, other transmission instrument mentioned in subsection (1), board,     metal plate or painted marker.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_42__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may render less effective, inoperative, inaccessible, obstruct or tamper and interfere with a fire hydrant.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_42__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1), (2), (3), (4) and (5) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_4__part_C" data-eId="chp_4__part_C"><h2>Part C  Emergency evacuation plans</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_43" data-eId="sec_43"><h3>43. Chief Fire Officer may designate <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_43__term_1" data-eId="sec_43__term_1">premises</span> for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_43__term_2" data-eId="sec_43__term_2">emergency</span> evacuation plans</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_43__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_43__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span> may by written notice designate any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_43__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_1__term_2">premises</span> as <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_43__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_1__term_3">premises</span> requiring an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency_evacuation_plan" id="sec_43__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_1__term_4">emergency evacuation plan</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_43__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The notice contemplated in subsection (1), must be served on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_43__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_2__term_1">premises</span> concerned and addressed to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_43__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_2__term_2">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_43__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_2__term_3">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_43__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_43__subsec_2__term_4">premises</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_44" data-eId="sec_44"><h3>44. Duties of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_44__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupier" id="sec_44__term_2" data-eId="sec_44__term_2">occupier</span> of designated <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_44__term_3" data-eId="sec_44__term_3">premises</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_44__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">owner</span>, or with the approval of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">chief fire officer</span>, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupier" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">occupier</span>, of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__term_4">premises</span> designated in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_37" href="#sec_37">section 37</a> must</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">prepare a comprehensive <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency_evacuation_plan" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">emergency evacuation plan</span> for the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">premises</span> in accordance with the guideline contained in schedule 1 and submit it to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_3">chief fire officer</span> in            triplicate within 30 days of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_4" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_4">service</span> of the designation notice;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">establish a fire protection committee comprised of occupiers of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">premises</span> to assist the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_3">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_4" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_4">premises</span> to organise a fire protection                programme and regular and scheduled fire evacuation drills;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">ensure that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency_evacuation_plan" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__term_1">emergency evacuation plan</span> is reviewed</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">at least every 12 months;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">whenever the floor layout of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__term_1">premises</span> is changed; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">whenever the Chief Fire Officer requires revision of the plan;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">ensure that an up-to-date <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency_evacuation_plan" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">emergency evacuation plan</span>, any fire protection programmes, evacuation drills and any related documents are kept, maintained and all times               available in a control room on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_2">premises</span> for inspection by any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_3" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_3">member</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">display the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency_evacuation_plan" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1">emergency evacuation plan</span> at conspicuous positions inside the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_2">premises</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">identify a place of safety off the designated <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_1">premises</span>, but in the immediate vicinity of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_2">premises</span>, where persons who reside or work on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_3" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_3">premises</span> may gather during         an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_4" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_4">emergency</span> for the purpose of compiling a list of survivors.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_44__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span> may in respect of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">premises</span> designated in terms of section 37</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">require the review of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency_evacuation_plan" id="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">emergency evacuation plan</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_3">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_4" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_4">premises</span> and may provide directions in this regard;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">instruct the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_3">premises</span> to implement a fire protection program that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_4" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_4">chief fire officer</span> believes is necessary to ensure the safety of           persons and property on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_5" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_5">premises</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">require the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_2">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_3" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_3">premises</span> to provide the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_4" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_4">chief fire officer</span> with a certified copy of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency_evacuation_plan" id="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_5" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_5">emergency evacuation plan</span> and any associated                 documents at a specified time and place.</span></span></span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_4__part_D" data-eId="chp_4__part_D"><h2>Part D  Public gatherings</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_45" data-eId="sec_45"><h3>45. Prevention and control of overcrowding</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Prior to the usage of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_45__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__term_1">premises</span> for entertainment or public assembly, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_45__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__term_2">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_45__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__term_3">person in charge</span> of such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_45__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__term_4">premises</span> must submit an application for a population certificat     e to the controlling authority, as <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed" id="sec_45__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__term_5">prescribed</span> in Schedule 2 of this By-law.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The controlling authority may request additional information from the applicant.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding the provision in subsection (1), the controlling authority may instruct the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_45__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_3__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_45__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_3__term_2">person in
