charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_45__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_3__term_3">premises</span> to apply for either a temporary or a        permanent population certificate, should the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_45__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_3__term_4">premises</span> be used in respect of any other occupancy contemplated in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-National_Building_Regulations" id="sec_45__subsec_3__term_5" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_3__term_5">National Building Regulations</span> (A20).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A temporary population certificate is valid for a period not exceeding 30 calendar days.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The controlling authority must refuse to issue the temporary or permanent population certificate if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_45__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_5__term_1">premises</span> do not comply with the requirements of the National Building     Regulations (T1), and where the controlling authority is of the opinion that the non- compliance of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_45__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_5__term_2">premises</span> can be remedied, he must instruct the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_45__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_5__term_3">owner</span> or person in         charge of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_45__subsec_5__term_4" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_5__term_4">premises</span> in writing, to take all reasonable steps to render the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_45__subsec_5__term_5" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_5__term_5">premises</span> safe prior to the usage of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_45__subsec_5__term_6" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_5__term_6">premises</span> and the issuing of the temporary or permanent      population certificate.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If at any time the controlling authority becomes aware that the usage of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_45__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_6__term_1">premises</span> is not in accordance with the temporary or permanent population certificate, he must act     in terms of sections 4(2), section 6 and section 7 of this By-law.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The temporary and permanent population certificate is valid only for the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_45__subsec_7__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_7__term_1">premises</span> or portion of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_45__subsec_7__term_2" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_7__term_2">premises</span> for which it was issued, and when changes of occupancy occur or      alterations are made to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_45__subsec_7__term_3" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_7__term_3">premises</span> for which the certificate was issued, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_45__subsec_7__term_4" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_7__term_4">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_45__subsec_7__term_5" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_7__term_5">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_45__subsec_7__term_6" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_7__term_6">premises</span> must reapply for the certificate in accordance with      subsection (1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The temporary or permanent population certificate must be displayed in a clearly visible and conspicuous position in or on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_45__subsec_8__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_8__term_1">premises</span> for which the certificate was issued.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_9" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_9"><span class="akn-num">(9)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_45__subsec_9__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_9__term_1">owner</span> or the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_45__subsec_9__term_2" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_9__term_2">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_45__subsec_9__term_3" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_9__term_3">premises</span> must prevent overcrowding by limiting the maximum population to that which is specified on the temporary or permanent           population certificate.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_10" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_10"><span class="akn-num">(10)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A person must vacate the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_45__subsec_10__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_10__term_1">premises</span> that are overcrowded when instructed to do so by the controlling authority, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_45__subsec_10__term_2" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_10__term_2">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_45__subsec_10__term_3" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_10__term_3">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_45__subsec_10__term_4" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_10__term_4">premises</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_46" data-eId="sec_46"><h3>46. Attendance of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_46__term_1" data-eId="sec_46__term_1">service</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_46__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When the controlling authority is of the opinion that a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_46__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_1__term_1">service</span> is required to be in attendance during a function in a place used for entertainment or public assembly, he may     provide, in the interest of public safety and subject to the exigencies of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_46__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_1__term_2">service</span>, one or more members, a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_46__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_1__term_3">vehicle</span> or equipment of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_46__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_1__term_4">service</span> to be in attendance on the       <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_46__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_1__term_5">premises</span> for the duration of the function or part thereof.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_46__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When the attendance of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_46__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_2__term_1">service</span> during a function in a place used for entertainment or public assembly involves costs, the costs incurred by the Municipality may be             recovered from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_46__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_2__term_2">person in charge</span> of the function in accordance with section 25 of this By-law.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_47" data-eId="sec_47"><h3>47. Prohibition of public gatherings in certain circumstances</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_47__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may hold a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_gathering" id="sec_47__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_1__term_1">public gathering</span> or allow a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_gathering" id="sec_47__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_1__term_2">public gathering</span> to be held in any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_47__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_1__term_3">building</span> or temporary structure unless a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_fitness" id="sec_47__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_1__term_4">certificate of fitness</span> has been issued by the        <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_47__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_1__term_5">chief fire officer</span> in respect of that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_47__subsec_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_1__term_6">building</span> or temporary structure, unless a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_fitness" id="sec_47__subsec_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_1__term_7">certificate of fitness</span> previously issued in terms of this subsection, has not yet expired.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_47__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Subsection (1) does not apply in respect of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">building</span> or temporary structure which existed at the commencement of this by-laws, unless after that date</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">building</span> or temporary structure is rebuilt, altered, extended or its floor layout is changed; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">ownership or control of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">building</span> or structure changes.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_47__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_48" data-eId="sec_48"><h3>48. Application for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_fitness" id="sec_48__term_1" data-eId="sec_48__term_1">certificate of fitness</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_48__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_48__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_1__term_1">owner</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_48__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_1__term_2">building</span> or temporary structure intended for the holding of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_gathering" id="sec_48__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_1__term_3">public gathering</span> must complete and submit to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_48__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_1__term_4">chief fire officer</span> an application form for a      <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_fitness" id="sec_48__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_1__term_5">certificate of fitness</span> in the form and manner as contemplated in section 42.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_48__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An application contemplated in subsection (1) must be submitted at least 30 days before any intended <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_gathering" id="sec_48__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__term_1">public gathering</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_48__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_49" data-eId="sec_49"><h3>49. Requirements for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_fitness" id="sec_49__term_1" data-eId="sec_49__term_1">certificate of fitness</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_49__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span> may not issue a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_fitness" id="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">certificate of fitness</span> in respect of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">building</span> or temporary structure</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">unless the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">municipality</span> is in possession of an up-to-date set of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">building</span> plans for the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_3">premises</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">unless the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">building</span> or temporary structure complies with the requirements of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">this by-law</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_49__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">for a period of validity exceeding 12months.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_50" data-eId="sec_50"><h3>50. Form and content of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_fitness" id="sec_50__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__term_1">certificate of fitness</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_50__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_fitness" id="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">certificate of fitness</span> must be in the form as <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed" id="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">prescribed</span> and must at least record the following information, where applicable</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the trade name and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-street" id="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">street</span> address of each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupier" id="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">occupier</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_3">building</span> or temporary structure;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a description of the type of activity carried on by each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupier" id="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">occupier</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">building</span> or structure;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the full names and addresses of the persons who serve on the governing or similar body of each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupier" id="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">occupier</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the maximum permissible number of people who may be admitted to the useable floor area of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">building</span> or structure;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">the number of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1">emergency</span> exits and their dimensions; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">the dates of issue and expiry of the certificate and its serial number.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_50__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding subsection (1), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_50__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__subsec_2__term_1">chief fire officer</span> may request additional information from the applicant.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_51" data-eId="sec_51"><h3>51. Duties of holder of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_fitness" id="sec_51__term_1" data-eId="sec_51__term_1">certificate of fitness</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_51__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The holder of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_fitness" id="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">certificate of fitness</span> must</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">comply with the provisions of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_fitness" id="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">certificate of fitness</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">at all times</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">display the certificate prominently on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_1">premises</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">maintain the certificate in a legible condition;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">immediately notify the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">chief fire officer</span> in writing of any change to the trade name, activity or governing or similar body of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupier" id="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2">occupier</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_3" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_3">building</span> or structure;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">submit any application for renewal of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_fitness" id="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">certificate of fitness</span> at least 30 days before its expiry in the form and manner <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed" id="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_2">prescribed</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_51__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_51__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_52" data-eId="sec_52"><h3>52. Cancellation of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_fitness" id="sec_52__term_1" data-eId="sec_52__term_1">certificate of fitness</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_52__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span> may cancel any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_fitness" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">certificate of fitness</span> in respect of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">premises</span> or temporary structure if he has reason to believe that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_3">premises</span> concerned contravenes or fails to comply with any provision of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_4" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_4">this by-law</span>; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">building</span> or structure does not comply with the requirements of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">this by-law</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_52__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Subject to subsection (3), before the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span> cancels a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_fitness" id="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">certificate of fitness</span> as contemplated in subsection (1), he must</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">give the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_3">premises</span> written notice of the intention to cancel the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_fitness" id="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_4" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_4">certificate of fitness</span> and the reasons for such cancellation;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">give the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_3">premises</span> a period of at least 21 days to make written representations regarding the matter to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_4" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_4">municipality</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_52__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_52__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_3__term_1">chief fire officer</span> has reason to believe that the failure to cancel a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_fitness" id="sec_52__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_3__term_2">certificate of fitness</span> may endanger any person or property, he may cancel a certificate of           fitness without prior notice to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_52__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_3__term_3">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_52__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_3__term_4">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_52__subsec_3__term_5" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_3__term_5">premises</span> as contemplated in subsection (2).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_52__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span> cancels a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_fitness" id="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__term_2">certificate of fitness</span> in terms of subsection (3), he must</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">furnish the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_2">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_3">premises</span> or temporary structure concerned with written notice of the cancellation;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">give the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_2">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_3">premises</span> a period of at least 21 days to make written representations regarding the matter to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_4" data-eId="sec_52__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_4">municipality</span>.</span></span></span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_4__part_E" data-eId="chp_4__part_E"><h2>Part E  Safety at Events</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_53" data-eId="sec_53"><h3>53. Submission of applications for approval to hold or stage events</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_53__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_53__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An application to hold or stage an event must be made by the event organiser and submitted </span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_53__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">by a person who is at least 18 years old;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_53__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">in a form as <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed" id="sec_53__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">prescribed</span> by the Chief Fire Officer;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_53__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">within the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed" id="sec_53__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">prescribed</span> time frames; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_53__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">by a person or on behalf of a person who possesses the necessary capacity and resources, as set out in the schedule 3, to the controlling authority.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_53__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The application must include all information required as indicated in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed" id="sec_53__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_2__term_1">prescribed</span> form and any additional information as may be requested by the controlling authority.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_53__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_53__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In the event of failure to submit the information referred to in subsection (2) an application will not be considered in terms of this By-Law.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_54" data-eId="sec_54"><h3>54. Requirements and conditions</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_54__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may hold or stage any event without obtaining a permit referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_60" href="#sec_60">section 60</a>(1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_54__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An application for an event must comply with the provisions of this By-law and contain such information as indicated in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed" id="sec_54__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_2__term_1">prescribed</span> application form.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_54__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The event organizer may not advertise the planned event before an application is submitted to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_54__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_3__term_1">municipality</span> and the controlling authority has informed the event organizer     that the application has been <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approved" id="sec_54__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_3__term_2">approved</span> in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_60" href="#sec_60">section 60</a>(1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_54__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_54__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_4__term_1">chief fire officer</span> must, depending on the nature of the event, ensure that consultation with relevant stakeholders identified by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_54__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_4__term_2">municipality</span> is undertaken by the        event organizer.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_54__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Council must, as part of its budgeting process in terms of the Local Government: Municipal Finance Management Act, 2003 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/2003/56" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/2003/56">Act No. 56 of 2003</a>), determine     tariffs and deposit payable for events.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_54__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_54__subsec_6__list_1" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_6__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_54__subsec_6__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_6__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> shall not, in respect of any planning for an event, application, approval or permit issued for an event in terms of this By-law, be held liable for any </span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_54__subsec_6__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_6__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">damage to or loss of any property of the event organiser; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_54__subsec_6__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_6__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">costs incurred by an event organiser or any third party.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_54__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The event organiser, or the venue <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_54__subsec_7__term_1" data-eId="sec_54__subsec_7__term_1">owner</span> in the case of a small event referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_59" href="#sec_59">section 59</a>(2)(b), shall be liable for the cost of any service provided by      the municipality for or in respect of an event.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_55" data-eId="sec_55"><h3>55. Decisions on events</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_55__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Chief Fire Officer must approve or decline an application for an event in terms of this By- Law.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_55__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where an application for an event has been <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approved" id="sec_55__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_2__term_1">approved</span>, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_55__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_2__term_2">chief fire officer</span> must issue a permit with conditions.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_55__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where an application for an event has been declined, reasons for the decision must be communicated to the applicant in writing.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_55__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_55__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The event organizer must make sure that the permit is available at the venue for inspection at all stages and at all times of the event.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_56" data-eId="sec_56"><h3>56. Holding of an event</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_56__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_56__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_56__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_56__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Event organisers whose applications have been <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approved" id="sec_56__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_56__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">approved</span> in terms of this By-law are responsible for the event and must ensure that </span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_56__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_56__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the event is held in compliance with the provisions of this By-law and does not contravene any other law;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_56__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_56__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the conduct of persons attending an event and the activities undertaken or carried out at the event do not negatively impact on affected communities during such event;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_56__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_56__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">any compliance notice issued by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_56__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_56__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">chief fire officer</span> in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_66" href="#sec_66">section 66</a> is complied with.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_57" data-eId="sec_57"><h3>57. Suspension and revocation of permit</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_57__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The Chief Fire Officer, may, where the event organizer fails to comply with a compliance notice issued in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_65" href="#sec_65">section 65</a>, by notice in writing to the         event organizer </span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">suspend the permit immediately until the event organizer has complied with the compliance notice;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">revoke the permit and take such steps as may be necessary in terms of this By-law, and the event organizer shall be liable for any costs incurred thereby; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_57__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">on receipt of information relating to failure to comply with a compliance notice, suspend or revoke the permit of an event organizer.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_58" data-eId="sec_58"><h3>58. Indemnity</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_58__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_58__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_58__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_58__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The event organizer must provide </span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_58__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_58__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">evidence, to the satisfaction of the Municipal Manager, of appropriate indemnity cover; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_58__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_58__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">where an activity which may put the public at risk will be involved, evidence to the satisfaction of the Chief Fire Officer of appropriate specialized risk insurance,            blanket liability or work cover must be provided.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_58__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_58__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_58__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_58__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span> shall not be liable for any costs, including any damage or loss, incurred or suffered as a result of an event held without an approval in terms of this By       -law.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_59" data-eId="sec_59"><h3>59. Offences and Penalties</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_59__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Failure to comply with any provision of this By-Law constitutes an offence.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_59__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_59__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A person who commits an offence in terms of this By-Law shall, on conviction, be liable for a fine or a term of imprisonment, or both such fine and such imprisonment.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_4__part_F" data-eId="chp_4__part_F"><h2>Part F  Water supply for fire-fighting purposes</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_60" data-eId="sec_60"><h3>60. Township development water supply requirements</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_60__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every person who develops or redevelops a township must design and develop that township with a sufficient water supply, minimum fire flow and hydrant requirements as            contemplated in section 11 of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_60__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_1__term_1">SANS</span> 10090 and must furnish written proof of such compliance to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_60__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_1__term_2">chief fire officer</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_60__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_60__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every person who develops or redevelops a township must ensure that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_60__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the storage capacity and rate of replenishment of the reservoirs supplying water to the township are sufficient for the fire-fighting purposes contemplated in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_60__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">this by-law</span>         ;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_60__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the water supply from these reservoirs is reticulated in a manner that ensures that the water supply to any area in the township can be provided from at least two                directions; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_60__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">double supply mains are installed from the water supply source to the distribution reservoirs and double pumps are installed for the delivery of the water supply.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_60__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_60__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Subsection (2)(c) is deemed to be satisfied, if</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_60__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the water is supplied to the township from more than one reservoir;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_60__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">each reservoir receives water from a separate supply main and pump; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_60__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the reservoirs are connected to each other.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_60__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_60__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every person who develops or redevelops a township must ensure that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_60__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the water distribution system is designed and equipped with control valves positioned so that it is not necessary to close off any branch or any portion of the distributi         on system for more than 150 metres in any high risk area or for more than 300 metres in any moderate or low risk area in the event that the system, excluding any of the          branches, is damaged or requires repair; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_60__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if the redevelopment of any township alters the fire risk category of any area in the township as contemplated in section 48, the water reticulation system is adapted            without delay so as to comply with the requirements of sections 46 and 47.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_60__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_60__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_5__term_1">chief fire officer</span> must inspect fire hydrants and conduct flow and pressure tests as contemplated in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_60__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_5__term_2">SANS</span> 10090.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_60__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_60__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1), (2), (3) and (4) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_61" data-eId="sec_61"><h3>61. Township development fire-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-extinguishing_stream" id="sec_61__term_1" data-eId="sec_61__term_1">extinguishing stream</span> requirements</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_61__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_61__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every person who develops or redevelops a township must ensure that the water supply provides a fire-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-extinguishing_stream" id="sec_61__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_61__hcontainer_1__term_1">extinguishing stream</span> that is immediately available to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_61__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_61__hcontainer_1__term_2">service</span> in an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_61__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_61__hcontainer_1__term_3">emergency</span>, of the following volume and duration:</span><table id="sec_61__hcontainer_1__table_1" data-eId="sec_61__hcontainer_1__table_1">
<tr>
<th><span class="akn-p">Fire risk category</span></th>
<th><span class="akn-p">Fire risk category <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-extinguishing_stream" id="sec_61__hcontainer_1__table_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_61__hcontainer_1__table_1__term_1">extinguishing stream</span>(litres per minute)</span></th>
<th><span class="akn-p">Minimum volume of Minimum duration of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-extinguishing_stream" id="sec_61__hcontainer_1__table_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_61__hcontainer_1__table_1__term_2">extinguishing stream</span> (hours)</span></th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">High risk</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">11 500</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">6</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">Moderate risk</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">5 750</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">4</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">Low risk</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">2 300</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">2</span></td>
</tr>
</table></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_62" data-eId="sec_62"><h3>62. Township development fire hydrant requirements</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_62__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_62__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every person who develops or redevelops a township must ensure that fire hydrants are plotted on a plan and installed in accordance with the following minimum delivery volumes and distance frequencies:</span><table id="sec_62__subsec_1__table_1" data-eId="sec_62__subsec_1__table_1">
<tr>
<th><span class="akn-p">Fire risk category</span></th>
<th><span class="akn-p">Minimum fire hydrant delivery volume measured at peak consumption (litres per minute)</span></th>
<th><span class="akn-p">Minimum distance between fire hydrants (metres)</span></th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">High risk</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">1980</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">120</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">Moderate risk</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">1150</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">180</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">Low risk</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">900</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">240</span></td>
</tr>
</table></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_62__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_62__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every person who develops or redevelops a township must ensure that the position of fire hydrants is plotted accurately on a plan that is furnished to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_62__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_62__subsec_2__term_1">chief fire officer</span> for      operational fire-fighting purposes.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_63" data-eId="sec_63"><h3>63. Fire risk categories</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_63__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">For purposes of sections 46 and 47, the following areas of a township must be regarded</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">as high risk</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">any factory area, high density shopping area, warehouse or commercial <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_1">building</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">any plantation, timber yard or wooden <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_1">building</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii__term_1" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii__term_1">building</span> higher than 3 storeys;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iv__term_1" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iv__term_1">building</span> in which hazardous substances are used, handled or stored or in which hazardous processes are conducted; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_v" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">any other area that has a high fire risk or high fire spread risk;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">as moderate risk</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__list_1" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">any area in which</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_aa" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_aa"><span class="akn-num">(aa)</span><span class="akn-p">factories, commercial buildings or residential buildings are generally detached from each other and do not exceed 3 storeys; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_bb" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_bb"><span class="akn-num">(bb)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_bb__term_1" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_bb__term_1">chief fire officer</span> has not declared the materials processed or stored in these buildings as highly dangerous;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">any area where the fire risk and spread risk of fire is moderate; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">any other area that is not a high or low risk area; and</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">as low risk</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">any area that is mainly residential or semi-rural;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">any area that has predominantly detached, duet, cluster or town house developments; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_63__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">any area where the fire risk or risk of spread of fire is slight or insignificant.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_64" data-eId="sec_64"><h3>64. Connections to water reticulation system</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_64__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may obtain a water connection to the water reticulation system of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_64__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> unless the fire protection plans for the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_64__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_1__term_2">premises</span> to be connected have been          <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approved" id="sec_64__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_1__term_3">approved</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_64__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_1__term_4">chief fire officer</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_64__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every person or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">owner</span> of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">premises</span> who requires a water connection to the water reticulation system of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__term_3">municipality</span> must</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__term_1">premises</span> to be connected are protected by a sprinkler installation, ensure that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the connection is calculated and designed for each sprinkler installation in accordance with a rational design as contemplated in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-National_Building_Regulations" id="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_1">National Building Regulations</span>,              and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">the size, delivery pressure and flow of the water connection is calculated in advance by the responsible engineer;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">chief fire officer</span> requires a larger water connection for purposes of fire-fighting, provide the larger water connection;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">ensure that the size, work pressure and delivery flow, except in the case of a water connection to a sprinkler installation, is calculated and designed in accordance with         <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">SANS</span> 0400 (Part W); and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">ensure that the water installation upon completion complies with the provisions of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1">SANS</span>-1:1994.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_64__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_64__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_4__part_G" data-eId="chp_4__part_G"><h2>Part G  Prevention of fire hazards</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_65" data-eId="sec_65"><h3>65. Certain fires prohibited</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_65__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may make or allow any other person to make a fire that may endanger any person, animal or property.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_65__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_65__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No person may burn or allow any other person to burn any refuse or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-combustible_material" id="sec_65__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">combustible material</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">without the prior written permission of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_65__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">chief fire officer</span>; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">unless the refuse or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-combustible_material" id="sec_65__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">combustible material</span> is burnt in an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approved" id="sec_65__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2">approved</span> incinerating device.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_65__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person, who makes a fire or allows any other person to make a fire, must take reasonable steps to ensure that the fire does not endanger any person, animal or property.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_65__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The prohibition in subsection (2) does not apply to any fire made</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">in an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approved" id="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1">approved</span> and purpose-made stove, fireplace or hearth that forms an integrated part of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_2">building</span> or structure;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">for the purpose of preparing food on private <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1">premises</span> set aside for that purpose; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">in any device for preparing food which</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">is heated by electricity or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-liquefied_petroleum_gas" id="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__term_1">liquefied petroleum gas</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">is so positioned that the fire does not endanger any person, animal or property.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_65__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_65__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1), (2), (3) and (4) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_66" data-eId="sec_66"><h3>66. Storage and accumulation of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-combustible_material" id="sec_66__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__term_1">combustible material</span> prohibited</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_66__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may store any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-combustible_material" id="sec_66__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_1__term_1">combustible material</span> or allow it to be stored, at any place or in any manner that may pose a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_hazard" id="sec_66__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_1__term_2">fire hazard</span> to any person, animal or property.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_66__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may allow the accumulation of dust at any place in quantities sufficient to pose a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_hazard" id="sec_66__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_2__term_1">fire hazard</span> to any person, animal or property.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_66__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_66__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_3__term_1">use</span> or allow to be used any sawdust or similar <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-combustible_material" id="sec_66__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_3__term_2">combustible material</span> to soak up any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_liquid" id="sec_66__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_3__term_3">flammable liquid</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_66__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may allow soot or any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-combustible_material" id="sec_66__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_4__term_1">combustible material</span> to accumulate in any chimney, flue or duct in such quantities or in any manner that may pose a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_hazard" id="sec_66__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_4__term_2">fire hazard</span> to any      person or property.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_66__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may allow any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vegetation" id="sec_66__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_5__term_1">vegetation</span> to become overgrown at any place under that persons control that may pose a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_hazard" id="sec_66__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_5__term_2">fire hazard</span> to any person, animal or property.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_66__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_66__subsec_6__list_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_6__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_hazard" id="sec_66__subsec_6__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_6__list_1__term_1">fire hazard</span> contemplated in subsection (5) arises, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_66__subsec_6__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_6__list_1__term_2">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_66__subsec_6__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_6__list_1__term_3">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_66__subsec_6__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_6__list_1__term_4">premises</span> must without delay eliminate the hazard or cause the hazard to be           eliminated by</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_6__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_6__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">cutting any grass, leaves or weeds associated with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_hazard" id="sec_66__subsec_6__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_6__list_1__item_a__term_1">fire hazard</span> to a maximum height of 150 millimetres;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_6__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_6__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">pruning, chopping down or sawing any shrub or tree; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_66__subsec_6__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_6__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">removing any resulting combustible residue from the property.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_66__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_66__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1), (2), (3), (4), (5) and (6) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_67" data-eId="sec_67"><h3>67.
