Electrical fittings, equipment and appliances</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_67__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No person may cause or allow</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">any electrical supply outlet to be overloaded; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">any electrical appliance or extension lead to be used in any manner that may pose a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_hazard" id="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">fire hazard</span> to any person or property.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_67__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_67__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_68" data-eId="sec_68"><h3>68. Flame-emitting devices</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_68__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_68__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_68__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_68__subsec_1__term_1">use</span> or cause or allow the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_68__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_68__subsec_1__term_2">use</span> of any flame-emitting device, including but not limited to any candle, lantern or torch, in any manner that may pose a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_hazard" id="sec_68__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_68__subsec_1__term_3">fire hazard</span>     to any person or property.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_68__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_68__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_69" data-eId="sec_69"><h3>69. Discard of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_liquid" id="sec_69__term_1" data-eId="sec_69__term_1">flammable liquid</span> or substance in sewers or drains</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_69__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_69__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may discard into, or cause, permit or allow a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_liquid" id="sec_69__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_69__subsec_1__term_1">flammable liquid</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_69__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_69__subsec_1__term_2">flammable substance</span> to enter any waste or foul water or storm water sewer or drain whether            underground or on the surface.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_69__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_69__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A person who becomes aware of any escape, whether accidental or otherwise, of any quantity of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_liquid" id="sec_69__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_69__subsec_2__term_1">flammable liquid</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_69__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_69__subsec_2__term_2">flammable substance</span> which is likely to constitute a fire        hazard, from any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_69__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_69__subsec_2__term_3">premises</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_69__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_69__subsec_2__term_4">vehicle</span> into any sewer or drain or any inlet or drain linking with such sewer or drain, must immediately report such escape to the chief fire        officer.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_69__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_69__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1) and (2) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_70" data-eId="sec_70"><h3>70. Flammable gas</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_70__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may fill any balloon or other device with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_gas" id="sec_70__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_1__term_1">flammable gas</span> without the written authority of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_70__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_1__term_2">chief fire officer</span>, and subject to such conditions as he may require       after having regard to the circumstances of the specific case.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_70__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_70__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_71" data-eId="sec_71"><h3>71. Smoking restrictions and discarding of combustibles</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_71__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If conditions exist where smoking may create a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_hazard" id="sec_71__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_1__term_1">fire hazard</span> on any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_71__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_1__term_2">premises</span>, smoking must be prohibited and "No Smoking" signs complying with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_71__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_1__term_3">SANS</span> 1186: Part 1, must be           prominently displayed in positions as directed by the controlling authority.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_71__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A person may not remove or damage a "No Smoking" sign.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_71__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may light or smoke a cigarette or any other smoking materials or ignite or otherwise set fire to other material, nor hold or discard any lit or smouldering             substance in any place where expressly prohibited.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_71__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_71__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_4__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_71__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_4__term_2">person in charge</span> of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_71__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_4__term_3">premises</span> may not allow or permit any person to light or smoke a cigarette or any other smoking materials or ignite or otherwise set fire     to any other material, nor hold or discard any lit or smouldering substance in any place where expressly prohibited.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_71__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where smoking is permitted, adequate provision must be made for the safe disposal of any smoking materials and matches.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_71__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may discard or otherwise dispose of a burning cigarette or any other burning materials or objects including materials capable of self-ignition or capable of            spontaneous combustion, on any road, in any road reserve or in any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_place" id="sec_71__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_6__term_1">public place</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_71__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where any cigarette, smoking materials or other burning materials, including materials capable of self-ignition or spontaneous combustion are discarded from a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_71__subsec_7__term_1" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_7__term_1">vehicle</span> onto a     road, or in any road reserve or any other place, it shall be presumed, in the absence of evidence to the contrary, that such action was performed by the driver of such           <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_71__subsec_7__term_2" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_7__term_2">vehicle</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_71__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_71__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes the provisions of this section commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_72" data-eId="sec_72"><h3>72. Safety fire-breaks required</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_72__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Subject to the provisions of the National Veld and Forest Fire Act, 1998, (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1998/101" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1998/101">Act No. 101 of 1998</a>), every owner or occupier of an agricultural holding or        farm must clear and maintain a safety fire-break along every boundary of the agricultural holding or farm.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_72__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an obstruction occurs within the boundaries of a safety fire-break, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_72__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_2__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupier" id="sec_72__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_2__term_2">occupier</span> concerned must clear and maintain a 5metre-wide safety fire-break around that        obstruction.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_72__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may clear or maintain a safety fire-break by burning without the prior written permission of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_72__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_3__term_1">chief fire officer</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_72__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_72__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any person who intends to clear or maintain a safety fire-break by burning must</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">apply in writing to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_72__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1">chief fire officer</span> for permission, stipulating the property concerned and the proposed date and time of the burning; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_72__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">unless the burning is to be performed by a person or body accredited for this purpose by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_72__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1">municipality</span>, request the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_72__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_2">service</span> to provide assistance at the burning.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_72__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_72__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1), (2), (3) and (4) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_5" data-eId="chp_5"><h2>Chapter 5<br>Regulation of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks" id="chp_5__term_1" data-eId="chp_5__term_1">fireworks</span>
</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_73" data-eId="sec_73"><h3>73. Designation of places and conditions</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_73__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_73__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> may designate any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_place" id="sec_73__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_1__term_2">public place</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-street" id="sec_73__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_1__term_3">street</span> or any part thereof within the municipal area as the only place at which <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks" id="sec_73__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_1__term_4">fireworks</span> may be discharged.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_73__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_73__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span> may, on application of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_73__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_2__term_2">owner</span> or lawful <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupier" id="sec_73__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_2__term_3">occupier</span> of any private open space as defined in the applicable zoning scheme regulations in its area of jurisdict     ion, designate such private open space as a place where <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks" id="sec_73__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_2__term_4">fireworks</span> may be discharged.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_73__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The list of places designated in terms of subsections (1) and (2) or any amendment thereof must be published by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_73__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_3__term_1">municipality</span> in terms of its communication strategy.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_73__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_73__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_4__term_1">municipality</span> may impose conditions as to the dates on which, periods or time and hours when the discharge of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks" id="sec_73__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_4__term_2">fireworks</span> may take place on any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-designated_area" id="sec_73__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_4__term_3">designated area</span> and may          further impose conditions as to the manner of discharge.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_73__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_73__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A person who fails to comply with any condition imposed in terms of subsection (4) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_74" data-eId="sec_74"><h3>74. Discharge of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks" id="sec_74__term_1" data-eId="sec_74__term_1">fireworks</span>
</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_74__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_74__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-item" id="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">No person may discharge any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks" id="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">fireworks</span> outside an area designated by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">municipality</span> in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_59" href="#sec_59">section 59</a>.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">Any person who wishes to present a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks_display" id="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">fireworks display</span> must apply to the Chief Fire Officer for authorisation by completing and submitting an application in the form and           manner determined by the Municipality together with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed" id="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">prescribed</span> tariff and a sketch plan of the proposed venue for the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks_display" id="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_3">fireworks display</span>, including the demarcated area         for the discharge and fallout of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks" id="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_4" data-eId="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_4">fireworks</span>.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">The application, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed_fee" id="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">prescribed fee</span> and accompanying documentation must be submitted to the Chief Fire Officer at least 14 days before the date of the proposed <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks" id="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_74__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_2">fireworks</span>             display.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_75" data-eId="sec_75"><h3>75. Dealing in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks" id="sec_75__term_1" data-eId="sec_75__term_1">fireworks</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_75__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_75__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No person may deal in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks" id="sec_75__subsec_4__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_4__list_1__term_1">fireworks</span> unless</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_75__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">that person holds the required <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks" id="sec_75__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1">fireworks</span> licence in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Explosives_Act" id="sec_75__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_2">Explosives Act</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_75__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">has written authority from the Chief Fire Officer.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_75__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_75__subsec_5__list_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_5__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any person who wishes to obtain the written authority of the Chief Fire Officer to deal in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks" id="sec_75__subsec_5__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_5__list_1__term_1">fireworks</span> as contemplated in subsection (1) must</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_75__subsec_5__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_5__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">complete an application in the form and manner determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_75__subsec_5__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_5__list_1__item_a__term_1">municipality</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_75__subsec_5__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_5__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">submit it to the Chief Fire Officer together with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed_fee" id="sec_75__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__term_1">prescribed fee</span> at least 30 days before the authority is required by the applicant.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_75__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Chief Fire Officer may cancel any written authority to deal in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks" id="sec_75__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_6__term_1">fireworks</span> if the holder of the authority contravenes any provision of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_75__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_75__subsec_6__term_2">this by-law</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_76" data-eId="sec_76"><h3>76. Seizure of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks" id="sec_76__term_1" data-eId="sec_76__term_1">fireworks</span>
</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_76__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_76__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_76__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_76__hcontainer_1__term_1">member</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_76__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_76__hcontainer_1__term_2">service</span> may take into his possession any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fireworks" id="sec_76__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_76__hcontainer_1__term_3">fireworks</span> found by him in contravention of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_60" href="#sec_60">section 60</a>(1) and such fireworks must be dealt with in terms of the relevant provisions of the Criminal Procedure Act relating to seizure and disposal.</span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_6" data-eId="chp_6"><h2>Chapter 6<br>Certificate of registration for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="chp_6__term_1" data-eId="chp_6__term_1">use</span>, handling and storage of flammable substances</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_77" data-eId="sec_77"><h3>77. Use, handling and storage of flammable substances prohibited in certain circumstances</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_77__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Subject to the provisions of subsection (3), no person may <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_77__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_1__term_1">use</span>, handle or store any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_77__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_1__term_2">flammable substance</span> or allow such substance to be used, handled or stored on any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_77__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_1__term_3">premises</span>     unless that person is the holder of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_77__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_1__term_4">certificate of registration</span> issued by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_77__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_1__term_5">chief fire officer</span> in respect of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_77__subsec_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_1__term_6">flammable substance</span> and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_77__subsec_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_1__term_7">premises</span> concerned.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_77__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_77__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__term_2">flammable substance</span> concerned is of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-class" id="sec_77__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_2__term_3">class</span> and does not exceed the quantity stipulated     in Schedule 2.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_77__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" substance to be used, handled or          stored on any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__term_4">premises</span>, unless the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__term_5">flammable substance</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">is used, handled or stored in a manner that ensures that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">no <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_1" id="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_2" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_2">flammable substance</span> fumes come into contact with any source of ignition that may cause the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_3" <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_1">emergency</span>, the escape of any person or animal is not hindered or obstructed in any way; or</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">is used, handled or stored</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">in a naturally ventilated room that prevents the accumulation of fumes or gas;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">in a suitable place outdoors that ensures the safe disposal of fumes or gas; or</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span strong, gas-tight and labelled</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_77__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_77__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1) and (3) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_78" data-eId="sec_78"><h3>78. <span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_78__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_78__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An application for a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_78__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_78__hcontainer_1__term_1">certificate of registration</span> contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_63" href="#sec_63">section 63</a>(1) must be completed and submitted in the form and manner prescribed.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_79" data-eId="sec_79"><h3>79. </h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_79__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_79__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_79__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the number of storage tanks or storage facilities on the <span class="akn-term" class="akn-item" id="sec_79__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the number of <span class="akn-term" capacities;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_79__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the number of installations, types of installations and the combined capacity of all cylinders that may be stored on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" facility;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_79__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">the period of validity and expiry date of the certificate; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_79__subsec_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_1__list_1__item_g"><span id="sec_79__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_79__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_79__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" writing.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_79__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_79__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_79__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">certificate of registration</span> is valid only for</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_79__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the installation for which it was issued;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_79__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the state of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_79__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">premises</span> at the time of issue; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_79__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_79__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">for the quantities of <span class="akn-term" certificate.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_80" data-eId="sec_80"><h3>80. </h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_80__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The holder of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_80__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_1__term_1">certificate of registration</span> must ensure that the certificate is available on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_80__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_1__term_2">premises</span> concerned at all times for inspection by any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_80__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_80__subsec_1__term_3">member</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_81" data-eId="sec_81"><h3>81. Fire-fighting equipment</h3>

extinguishers</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span (transportable-type);</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">require that a fire detection or warning system be installed.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_81__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span subsection (1)</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_81__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__list_1__term_1">chief fire 12months;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if adequately protected from the weather; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_81__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span not possible, the position of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_fighting_equipment" id="sec_81__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__list_1__term_1" officer</span>.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_81__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_81__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span data-eId="sec_82"><h3>82. Amendment to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_82__term_1" data-eId="sec_82__term_1">certificate of registration</span>
</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_82__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_82__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_82__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_82__hcontainer_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span> may amend any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_82__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_82__hcontainer_1__term_2">certificate of registration</span> on application by the holder.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_83" data-eId="sec_83"><h3>83. Cancellation of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_83__term_1" data-eId="sec_83__term_1">certificate of registration</span>
</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_83__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_83__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The provisions of section 44, read with the necessary changes, apply to any cancellation by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_83__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_83__hcontainer_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_83__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_83__hcontainer_1__term_2">certificate of registration</span>.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_84" data-eId="sec_84"><h3>84. Renewal of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_84__term_1" data-eId="sec_84__term_1">certificate of registration</span>
</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_84__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_84__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any application for the renewal of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_84__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_84__hcontainer_1__term_1">certificate of registration</span> must be submitted to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_84__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_84__hcontainer_1__term_2">chief fire officer</span> at least 30 days prior to the expiry date of the certificate.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_85" data-eId="sec_85"><h3>85. No authorisation required for certain motor <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_85__term_1" data-eId="sec_85__term_1">vehicle</span> fuel tanks</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_85__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_85__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_85__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_85__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_85__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_85__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">certificate of registration</span> contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_63" href="#sec_63">section 63</a>(1) or any other authorisation contemplated in this by-law is required in respect of flammable liquids in a fuel tank</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_85__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_85__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">of any motor <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_85__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_85__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">vehicle</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_85__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_85__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">of any stationery engine if the volume of the fuel tank does not exceed 1 000 litres.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_86" data-eId="sec_86"><h3>86. Record of certificates of registration</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_86__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_86__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_86__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_86__hcontainer_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span> must keep updated records of all <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_86__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_86__hcontainer_1__term_2">premises</span> in respect of which a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_86__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_86__hcontainer_1__term_3">certificate of registration</span> has been issued, amended or renewed.</span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_7" data-eId="chp_7"><h2>Chapter 7<br>General provisions regarding the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="chp_7__term_1" data-eId="chp_7__term_1">use</span>, handling and storage of flammable substances</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_87" data-eId="sec_87"><h3>87. General prohibitions regarding the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_87__term_1" data-eId="sec_87__term_1">use</span>, handling and storage of flammable substances</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_87__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_87__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No person who uses, handles or stores a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_87__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">flammable substance</span> or allows them to be used, handled or stored on any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_87__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">premises</span> may</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_87__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">do anything or allow anything to be done that may result in or cause a fire or explosion;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_87__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">do anything or allow anything to be done that may obstruct the escape to safety of any person or animal during an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_87__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">emergency</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_87__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No person may</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dump" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">dump</span> or spill or allow the dumping or spilling of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2">flammable substance</span> into any borehole, sewer, drain system or surface water;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">discard or allow the discarding of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">flammable substance</span> from any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2">premises</span> in any way other than by a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-competent_person" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_3">competent person</span> who is properly equipped and authorised to do in         terms of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_4" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_4">this by-law</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">make or bring any fire or device capable of producing an open flame or allow any other person to do so, within 5 metres of any place where a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">flammable substance</span> is stored         ;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1">use</span> or allow to be used any device in connection with a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_2">flammable substance</span> in any basement level of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_3" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_3">building</span>, other than a gas welding or cutting device, used for the         sole purpose of maintenance of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_4" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_4">building</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__list_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">while any person, except the driver or any other person responsible for a bus contemplated in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-National_Road_Traffic_Act" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_1">National Road Traffic Act</span>, is in or on the bus</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">fill or allow the filling of its fuel tank; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">transport or allow the transport of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii__term_1">flammable substance</span> on the bus, except in its fuel tank; and</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">deliver or supply or allow to be delivered or supplied, any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_1">flammable substance</span> to any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_2" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_2">premises</span> unless the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_3" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_3">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_4" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_4">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_5" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_5">premises</span> is in possession of a         valid <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_6" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_6">certificate of registration</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_87__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_87__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1) and (2) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_88" data-eId="sec_88"><h3>88. Use, handling and storage of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-liquefied_petroleum_gas" id="sec_88__term_1" data-eId="sec_88__term_1">liquefied petroleum gas</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_88__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No person may <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">use</span>, handle or store <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-liquefied_petroleum_gas" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">liquefied petroleum gas</span> in any quantity exceeding that stipulated in Schedule 2 unless</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the person is in possession of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">certificate of registration</span> contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_63" href="#sec_63">section 63</a>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">use</span>, handling and storage of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-liquefied_petroleum_gas" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">liquefied petroleum gas</span> complies with the requirements of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_3">SANS</span> 087, Parts 1, 3, 7 and 10.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_88__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Liquid petroleum gas may only be used, handled or stored within property boundaries and in compliance with safety distances stipulated in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_88__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_2__term_1">SANS</span> 087, Parts 1, 3, 7 and 10.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_88__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any storage of liquid petroleum gas cylinders at any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_88__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_3__term_1">service</span> station for retail purposes must comply with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_88__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_3__term_2">SANS</span> 087, Part 7.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_88__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No liquid petroleum gas cylinder may be used, handled or stored at any public exhibition or demonstration without the prior written permission of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_88__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_4__term_1">chief fire officer</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_88__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An application for permission contemplated in subsection (4) must be made in writing at least 14 days before the event concerned.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_88__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_88__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_6__term_1">chief fire officer</span> may impose any reasonable condition on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_88__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_6__term_2">use</span>, handling and storage of liquid petroleum gas cylinders at a public exhibition or demonstration,            including but not limited to, the number of cylinders, the manner of storage, safety distances and other safety requirements.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_88__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person using, handling or storing any liquid petroleum gas cylinder at any public exhibition or demonstration must comply with any condition imposed in terms of subsectio     n (6).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_88__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_88__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1), (2), (3), (4), (5), (6) and (7) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_89" data-eId="sec_89"><h3>89. Display of symbolic warning signs required</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_89__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_89__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_89__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_89__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">person in charge</span> of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_89__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">premises</span> where any flammable or explosive substance is used, handled or stored must, in the affected area of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_89__subsec_1__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_1__list_1__term_4">premises</span>, display           symbolic signs</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_89__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">prohibiting smoking and open flames;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_89__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">of a size and number determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_89__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">chief fire officer</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_89__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">prominently in places where the signs can be clearly observed.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_89__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may disregard or allow to be disregarded any prohibition on a symbolic sign displayed in terms of subsection (1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_89__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_89__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1) and (2) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_90" data-eId="sec_90"><h3>90. Duty to report fires, accidents and dumping</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_90__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_90__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If any fire, accident or dumping involving a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_90__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_90__subsec_1__term_1">flammable substance</span> has caused damage to any person, animal, property or the environment on any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_90__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_90__subsec_1__term_2">premises</span>, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_90__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_90__subsec_1__term_3">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupier" id="sec_90__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_90__subsec_1__term_4">occupier</span>      of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_90__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_90__subsec_1__term_5">premises</span> must immediately report it to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_90__subsec_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_90__subsec_1__term_6">chief fire officer</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_90__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_90__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_8" data-eId="chp_8"><h2>Chapter 8<br>Declaration of fire control zones and fire break burning seasons</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_91" data-eId="sec_91"><h3>91. Fire Control Zones</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_91__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where the Chief Fire Officer is of opinion that a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_control_zone" id="sec_91__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_1__term_1">fire control zone</span> should be declared in an area or that a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_control_zone" id="sec_91__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_1__term_2">fire control zone</span> should be disestablished, he or she must cause      such intention to be published in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_91__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_1__term_3">municipality</span>s public participation policy.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_91__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_91__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span> is of opinion that any objection or comment should be investigated, it may decide to hold a public enquiry.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_91__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_91__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_91__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> decides to hold a public inquiry, it must:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_91__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">appoint a suitably qualified person or panel of persons to hold such enquiry; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_91__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">determine the procedure for the public inquiry, which may include a public hearing.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_91__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The person or panel of persons appointed to hold such enquiry must conduct the inquiry in accordance with the procedure <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed" id="sec_91__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_4__term_1">prescribed</span> and compile a written report to the            relevant portfolio committee on the inquiry and give reasons for any administrative action recommended.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_91__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where practical, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_91__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_5__term_1">municipality</span> shall as soon as possible after the submission of the report to the relevant portfolio committee, publish a concise summary of such report      and the particulars of the places and times at which the report may be inspected and copied; and</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_91__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">After the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_91__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_6__term_1">municipality</span> has taken into account any comment or objection in respect of such proposed declaration or disestablishment it may declare a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_control_zone" id="sec_91__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_6__term_2">fire control zone</span> or          disestablish any such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_control_zone" id="sec_91__subsec_6__term_3" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_6__term_3">fire control zone</span> concerned.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_91__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_91__subsec_7__term_1" data-eId="sec_91__subsec_7__term_1">municipality</span> must publish such zone or amended zone.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_92" data-eId="sec_92"><h3>92. Firebreak Burning Seasons</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_92__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_92__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Chief Fire Officer may recommend the declaration of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-firebreak" id="sec_92__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_92__subsec_1__term_1">firebreak</span> burning seasons in which case the provisions of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_77" href="#sec_77">section 77</a>(1),(6) and (7) shall apply with       the necessary changes.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_9" data-eId="chp_9"><h2>Chapter 9<br>Storage of flammable substances</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_93" data-eId="sec_93"><h3>93. Storage of flammable substances prohibited in certain circumstances</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_93__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_93__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_93__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_93__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No person may store or allow the storage of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_93__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_93__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">flammable substance</span> in any storeroom unless</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_93__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_93__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">that person has a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_93__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_93__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">certificate of registration</span> contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_63" href="#sec_63">section 63</a>(1); and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_93__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_93__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the storeroom complies with the requirements of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_93__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_93__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">this by-law</span> and any other applicable law.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_93__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_93__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_94" data-eId="sec_94"><h3>94. Taking of samples in respect of flammable substances</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_94__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Whenever a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_94__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__term_1">member</span> inspects any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_94__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__term_2">premises</span> and suspects that a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_94__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__term_3">flammable substance</span> is used, handled or stored on such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_94__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__term_4">premises</span> without a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_94__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__term_5">certificate of registration</span> or other        authority as contemplated in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_94__subsec_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__term_6">this by-law</span>, such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_94__subsec_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_1__term_7">member</span> must take a sample of such substance for the purposes of analysis or examination.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_94__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any sample as contemplated in subsection (1) must taken in the presence of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__term_3">premises</span> and must</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">be divided into two equal parts;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">be sealed in similar containers; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">such containers must be marked with the following information</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the address of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__term_1">premises</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">the trade name of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__term_1">premises</span> or concern;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">the name and signature of the person in whose presence the sample was taken;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">the date and time the sample was taken; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_v" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">a description of the location on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_v__term_1" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_v__term_1">premises</span> where the sample was taken.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_94__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_94__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_94__subsec_3__term_1">chief fire officer</span> must within reasonable time submit any sample taken as contemplated in subsection (1) to an accredited institution for an analysis or examination and      written report on the findings.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_95" data-eId="sec_95"><h3>95. Symbolic safety signs must be displayed</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_95__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The holder of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">certificate of registration</span> for a storeroom to be used for any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">flammable substance</span> must ensure that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">symbolic safety signs prohibiting open flames and smoking are displayed in the storeroom</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">of a number determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_1">chief fire officer</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">of dimensions at least 290 millimetres by 200millimetres; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">manufactured in accordance with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii__term_1" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii__term_1">SANS</span> 1186;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the groups of flammable substances and their corresponding quantities which may be stored in the storeroom are indicated on the outside of every door to the storeroom in         red letters at least 75 millimetres high, against a white background.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_95__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_95__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_96" data-eId="sec_96"><h3>96. Construction of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_96__term_1" data-eId="sec_96__term_1">flammable substance</span> storerooms</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_96__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every storeroom must be designed and constructed according to the following criteria</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the storeroom floor must consist of concrete;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the storeroom walls must consist of material that has a fire resistance of at least 120minutes;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">the storeroom roof must consist of</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">reinforced concrete with a fire resistance of at least 120minutes;
