or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__list_1" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">any other non-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-combustible_material" id="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__list_1__term_1">combustible material</span>, if the storeroom</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__list_1__item_aa" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__list_1__item_aa"><span class="akn-num">(aa)</span><span class="akn-p">is not situated within 5 metres of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-boundary" id="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__list_1__item_aa__term_1" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__list_1__item_aa__term_1">boundary</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__list_1__item_aa__term_2" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__list_1__item_aa__term_2">premises</span>; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__list_1__item_bb" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__list_1__item_bb"><span class="akn-num">(bb)</span><span class="akn-p">adjoins a higher wall with no opening within 10 metres above and 5 metres on either side of the storeroom.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_96__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_96__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_97" data-eId="sec_97"><h3>97. Requirements for storeroom doors</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_97__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every storeroom must be equipped with a fire rated <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_door" id="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">fire door</span> that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">is manufactured and installed in accordance with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">SANS</span> 1253;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">opens to the outside;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">is equipped with a lock or locks <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approved" id="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">approved</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2">chief fire officer</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">is at all times capable of being opened from the inside of the storeroom without the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">use</span> of a key.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_97__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A storeroom must be equipped with two or more fire doors if the distance to be covered from any part in that storeroom to a door is 4 metres or more, in which case, the fire     doors must be installed as far from each other as is practicable in the circumstances.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_97__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_97__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Fire doors contemplated in subsections (1) and (2) must if installed on</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_97__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">external walls, be "B" <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-class" id="sec_97__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">class</span> fire doors; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_97__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">internal walls in communication within a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_97__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">building</span>, be "D" <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-class" id="sec_97__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2">class</span> fire doors.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_97__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_97__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1), (2) and (3) commits an offence</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_98" data-eId="sec_98"><h3>98. Requirements for storeroom windows</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_98__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_98__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every storeroom window frame must</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_98__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">consist of steel;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_98__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">have window panels of dimensions not exceeding 450 millimetres  450millimetres; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_98__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">be fitted with wire glass of a thickness not less than 8millimetres.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_98__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No storeroom window must be capable of being opened.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_98__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every storeroom window must be fitted to the external wall of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_98__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_3__term_1">building</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_98__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_98__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1), (2) and (3) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_99" data-eId="sec_99"><h3>99. Requirements for storeroom catch pits</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_99__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_99__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_99__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_99__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every storeroom must be designed and constructed so that its floor is recessed below the level of the door sill to form a catch pit</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_99__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_99__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">with a holding capacity at least equal to the total volume of hazardous substances capable of being stored in the storeroom, plus 10 percent; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_99__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_99__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_99__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_99__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">if required by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_99__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_99__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_99__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_99__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">covered at door sill level by a strong, stable, non-combustible and oxidation free floor grill; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_99__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_99__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">equipped, at its lowest level, with a non-corrosive drainage valve for cleaning purposes and product recovery.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_99__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_99__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The floor grill contemplated in subsection (i) must contain a suitably positioned access hatch for cleaning purposes.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_99__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_99__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1) and (2) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_100" data-eId="sec_100"><h3>100. Ventilation of storerooms</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_100__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_100__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every storeroom must be designed and constructed to ensure</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_100__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the effective ventilation of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_100__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">flammable substance</span> fumes;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_100__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">that fumes released from the storeroom into the open air will not come into contact with any source of ignition.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_100__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_100__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If the storeroom is designed and constructed for natural ventilation, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_100__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_100__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">person in charge</span> of the storeroom must ventilate the storeroom at a minimum cycle of 30 air     changes per hour by installing non-combustible airbricks</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_100__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">that are not less than 140 millimetres by 250 millimetres in extent, with non-corrosive gauze wire with a minimum opening diameter of 0.5 millimetres;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_100__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">that are provided in at least 3 external walls of the storeroom; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_100__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">that are positioned 100 millimetres above the level of the sill and 100 millimetres below the level of the roof and not more than 450 millimetres apart.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_100__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If the storeroom is designed and constructed for mechanical ventilation, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__term_2">person in charge</span> of the storeroom must equip it with a mechanical ventilation system</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">designed and installed for this purpose;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">with a flow rate of 0,5 meters/second across the store;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">with vanes that consist of a static-free material;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__list_1" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">that discharges through a vertical metal duct into the open air</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">not situated within 5 metres of any opening of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_i__term_1">building</span> or erf <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-boundary" id="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_i__term_2" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_i__term_2">boundary</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">terminating at least 1 metre above roof height or at least 3,6 meters above ground level, whichever is the greater;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">equipped with ventilators that are firmly attached to the inside of the walls of the storeroom and, in the case of bottom ventilators, as close as possible to the level          of the sill;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">with all ventilation or air duct openings in the external wall opposite the mechanical ventilator installed 100 millimetres above the level of the sill to ensure                 effective cross-ventilation; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_g__list_1" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_g__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">equipped with ducting material that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">is as short as possible in the circumstances and does not have sharp bends; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">is fitted with a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_damper" id="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_ii__term_1">fire damper</span> of at least 120 minutes fire resistance at any point where the ducting exits the storeroom, if ducting material is installed external to              the storeroom in communication with the remainder of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_ii__term_2" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_3__list_1__item_g__list_1__item_ii__term_2">building</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_100__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_100__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1), (2) and (3) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_101" data-eId="sec_101"><h3>101. Electrical equipment in storerooms</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_101__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">person in charge</span> of any storeroom must ensure that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">all electrical apparatus, fittings or switch gear used or installed in the storeroom are used or installed as contemplated in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">SANS</span> 0108;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">no switch gear, distribution box, fuse or other electrical equipment, except electrical equipment as contemplated in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_1">SANS</span> 0108, is situated</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">inside the storeroom; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">in any position where it may come into contact with any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1">flammable substance</span> fumes leaving the storeroom;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">any metal part, electrical fittings and device used in or in connection with the storeroom are earthed effectively to each other and to the ground;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">any mechanical ventilation system switch is situated outside the storeroom;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">any mechanical ventilation system is on at all times, except when the system is being repaired or replaced, in which case the system must be repaired or replaced without         delay; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">all electrical apparatus and fittings, except the mechanical ventilation system, are switched off when the storeroom is unattended.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_101__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any electrical installation in a storeroom may be installed and certified only by an electrician who is qualified and competent by virtue of his or her training and experienc     e.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_101__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_101__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_3__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_101__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_3__term_2">person in charge</span> of a storeroom must submit the certificate contemplated in subsection (2) to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_101__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_3__term_3">chief fire officer</span> for record purposes immediately after           installation contemplated in such subsection.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_101__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_101__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1), (2) and (3) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_102" data-eId="sec_102"><h3>102. Foam inlets required for certain storerooms</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_102__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_102__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_102__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_102__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_102__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_102__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_102__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_102__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">person in charge</span> of a storeroom that is used or intended to be used for storing more than 5000 litres of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_102__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_102__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">flammable substance</span> must ensure</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_102__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_102__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">that the storeroom is provided with a foam inlet consisting of a 65mm male instantaneous coupling and mild steel pipe work leading to the inside thereof; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_102__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_102__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">that the foam inlet is identified by a sign in block letters at least 100 millimetres high, displaying the words "foam inlet".</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_102__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_102__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_103" data-eId="sec_103"><h3>103. Shelving in storerooms</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_103__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_103__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_103__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_103__subsec_1__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_103__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_103__subsec_1__term_2">person in charge</span> of a flammable storeroom must ensure that any racking of shelving erected or installed in the storeroom is of non-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-combustible_material" id="sec_103__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_103__subsec_1__term_3">combustible material</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_103__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_103__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_104" data-eId="sec_104"><h3>104. Unauthorised <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_104__term_1" data-eId="sec_104__term_1">use</span> and entry of storerooms prohibited</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_104__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_104__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No person may</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">without the authority of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">person in charge</span>, enter or allow any other person to enter any flammable storeroom;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">use</span> any storeroom or allow it to be used for any purpose other than for the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">use</span>, handling or storage of flammable substances;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">allow any person to work in a storeroom unless all the doors of the storeroom are wide open or the mechanical ventilation system is switched on; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_104__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">place or allow to be placed any obstruction or hindrance in a passage of any storeroom or in front of any storeroom door.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_104__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_104__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_105" data-eId="sec_105"><h3>105. Mixing and decanting rooms</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_105__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_105__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_105__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_105__subsec_1__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_105__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_105__subsec_1__term_2">person in charge</span> of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_105__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_105__subsec_1__term_3">premises</span> where quantities of flammable liquids exceeding those stipulated in schedule 3 are decanted or mixed, must ensure that any room     where decanting or mixing takes place complies with all requirements of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_105__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_105__subsec_1__term_4">this by-law</span> applicable to storerooms.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_105__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_105__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_106" data-eId="sec_106"><h3>106. Temporary above ground storage of flammable substances</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_106__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person, who wishes to store any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_106__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_1__term_1">flammable substance</span> on <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_106__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_1__term_2">premises</span> on a temporary basis, must apply to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_106__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_1__term_3">chief fire officer</span> for a temporary <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_106__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_1__term_4">certificate of registration</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_106__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A temporary <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">certificate of registration</span> may be issued by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">chief fire officer</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">for a period not exceeding 12months;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_1">flammable substance</span> concerned is required</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">in respect of excavation work, construction work or road construction if the volume of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_1">flammable substance</span> does not exceed 9 000 litres;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">in respect of small fleet maintenance or research purposes, if the volume of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1">flammable substance</span> does not exceed 4 400 litres; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">the application complies with the requirements of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii__term_1" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii__term_1">SANS</span> 0131 and this Chapter.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_106__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every holder of a temporary <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">certificate of registration</span> contemplated in subsection (1) must ensure that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a storage tank for the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">flammable substance</span> is not erected within 3.5 metres of any erf <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-boundary" id="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_2">boundary</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_3">building</span>, excavation, road, driveway or any other flammable substances or         <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-combustible_material" id="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_4" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_4">combustible material</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">adequate provision is made for rainwater run-off from retaining walls or embankments;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">no source of ignition or potential source of ignition exists within 5 metres of a storage tank;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">a symbolic sign of dimensions at least 300 millimetres by 300 millimetres prohibiting smoking and open flames is displayed on every side of a temporary storage tank; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_3__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">at least two 9-kilogram dry chemical fire extinguishers are installed and kept in good working condition, within 10 metres of a temporary storage tank.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_106__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_106__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1), (2) and (3) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_107" data-eId="sec_107"><h3>107. Hand tools must be intrinsically safe</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_107__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_107__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_107__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_107__subsec_1__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_107__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_107__subsec_1__term_2">person in charge</span> of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_107__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_107__subsec_1__term_3">flammable substance</span> storeroom must ensure that any hand tool used in the storeroom is intrinsically safe.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_107__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_107__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_108" data-eId="sec_108"><h3>108. Permanent above ground storage tanks for flammable liquids</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_108__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">In addition to any other requirement of this Chapter, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">person in charge</span> of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-above_ground_storage_tank" id="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">above ground storage tank</span> for flammable liquids must ensure</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">that the tank is erected or installed</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">in accordance with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_1">SANS</span> 0131 and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_2" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_2">SANS</span> 089, Part I;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">at least 3.5 metres from any erf <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-boundary" id="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_1">boundary</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_2" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_2">building</span>, excavation, road, driveway or any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_3" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_3">flammable substance</span>, combustible substance or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-combustible_material" id="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_4" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_4">combustible material</span>;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_liquid" id="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">flammable liquid</span> stored in the tank must be clearly identified by means of Hazchem placards contemplated in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">SANS</span> 0232, Part 1.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_108__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any electrical installation associated with the storage tank must comply with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_108__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_2__term_1">SANS</span> 0108 and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_108__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_2__term_2">SANS</span> 089, Part 2.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_108__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_108__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1) and (2) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_109" data-eId="sec_109"><h3>109. Underground storage tanks for flammable liquids</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_109__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_109__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_1__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_109__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_1__term_2">person in charge</span> of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_109__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_1__term_3">premises</span> used or intended to be used for the underground storage of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_liquid" id="sec_109__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_1__term_4">flammable liquid</span> must ensure that any underground storage tank,      pump, dispenser and pipe work is erected or installed in accordance with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_109__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_1__term_5">SANS</span> 0400, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_109__subsec_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_1__term_6">SANS</span> 089, Part 3 and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_109__subsec_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_1__term_7">SANS</span> 0131.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_109__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_109__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_110" data-eId="sec_110"><h3>110. Installing, erecting, removing and demolishing prohibited without prior notice</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_110__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may, in respect of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-registered_premises" id="sec_110__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_1__term_1">registered premises</span>, erect, install, remove, demolish, extend or change any delivery pump, storage tank, storeroom, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-spraying_room" id="sec_110__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_1__term_2">spraying room</span>, gas installati     on, storage facility, fire protection arrangement or floor layout unless that person has given the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_110__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_1__term_3">chief fire officer</span> at least 3 working days prior written notice of the         intention to do so, in the form and manner as <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed" id="sec_110__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_1__term_4">prescribed</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_110__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The notice in term of subsection (1) must include the intended commencement date and estimated completion date of the proposed work.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_110__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_110__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The provisions of subsection (1) do not apply to</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_110__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the temporary removal of equipment for purposes of carrying out necessary repairs;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_110__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the necessary replacement of equipment or their parts; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_110__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the replacement of any storage tank with a tank of the same capacity.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_110__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_110__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) and (2) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_111" data-eId="sec_111"><h3>111. Repair and maintenance of access to storage tanks</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_111__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_111__subsec_7__list_1" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_7__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No person may enter or allow any other person to enter any storage tank that has at any time contained a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_111__subsec_7__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_7__list_1__term_1">flammable substance</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_111__subsec_7__list_1__item_1" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_7__list_1__item_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-p">until such tank has been de-aerated and made free of gas and fumes as contemplated in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_111__subsec_7__list_1__item_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_7__list_1__item_1__term_1">SANS</span> 089 (Part I); or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_111__subsec_7__list_1__item_2" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_7__list_1__item_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_111__subsec_7__list_1__item_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_7__list_1__item_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">unless that person</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_111__subsec_7__list_1__item_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_7__list_1__item_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">is wearing an effective self-supporting breathing apparatus; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_111__subsec_7__list_1__item_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_7__list_1__item_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">is attached to a rescue rope under the control of a competent and responsible person.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_111__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_111__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_112" data-eId="sec_112"><h3>112. Termination of storage and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_112__term_1" data-eId="sec_112__term_1">use</span> of flammable substances</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_112__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If an aboveground or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-underground_tank" id="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">underground tank</span> installation, liquid petroleum gas installation or associated pipe work is no longer required for the storage or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">use</span> of a flammable         substance, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__term_4">person in charge</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__term_5">premises</span> on which the installation is located, must</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">notify the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">chief fire officer</span> in writing within seven days of such storage or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">use</span> ceasing;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">ensure that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">flammable substance</span> is removed from the installation and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">premises</span> are rendered safe within 30 days of the cessation;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">unless the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">chief fire officer</span> directs otherwise, remove the installation including any associated pipe work from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2">premises</span> within 180 days of the cessation; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">to the satisfaction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">chief fire officer</span>, restore any public foot path or roadway that has been disturbed by the removal of the installation within a period of 7            days of completing such removal.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_112__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding the provisions of subsection (1) if the removal of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-underground_tank" id="sec_112__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_2__term_1">underground tank</span> installation for the storage of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_112__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_2__term_2">flammable substance</span> will detrimentally affect the       stability of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_112__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_2__term_3">premises</span> concerned, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_112__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_2__term_4">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_112__subsec_2__term_5" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_2__term_5">person in charge</span> of the installation may, with the prior written permission of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_112__subsec_2__term_6" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_2__term_6">chief fire officer</span>, fill the underground     tank with liquid cement slurry.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_112__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_112__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_113" data-eId="sec_113"><h3>113. Container handling and storage</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_113__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">flammable substance</span> container must</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">be kept closed when not in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">use</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">be declared gas- or vapour-free by a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-competent_person" id="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">competent person</span> before any modification or repairs are undertaken;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">be manufactured and maintained in such condition as to be reasonably safe from damage and to prevent leakage of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">flammable substance</span> or vapour from the container.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_113__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_liquid" id="sec_113__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_2__term_1">flammable liquid</span> container must be labelled and marked with words and details indicating the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_liquid" id="sec_113__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_2__term_2">flammable liquid</span> contained in the container as well as any hazard associate     d with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_liquid" id="sec_113__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_2__term_3">flammable liquid</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_113__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may extract <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_liquid" id="sec_113__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_3__term_1">flammable liquid</span> from a container of a capacity exceeding 200 litres, unless the container is fitted with an adequately sealed pump or tap.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_113__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any empty <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_liquid" id="sec_113__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_4__term_1">flammable liquid</span> container must be stored in a storeroom.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_113__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Notwithstanding the provisions of subsection (4) the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span> may permit the storage of any empty <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_liquid" id="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__term_2">flammable liquid</span> container in the open air if no storeroom is         available and if he is satisfied that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the storage area is in a position and of sufficient size that a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_hazard" id="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__item_a__term_1">fire hazard</span> or other threatening danger will not be caused;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the storage area is well ventilated and enclosed by a wire mesh fence;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the fence supports are of steel or reinforced concrete;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the storage area has an outward opening gate that is kept locked when not in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__item_d__term_1">use</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">when the floor area exceeds 10m an additional escape gate is installed and fitted with a sliding bolt or other similar locking device that can be opened from the inside         without the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__item_e__term_1">use</span> of a key; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">the storage area is free of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vegetation" id="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_5__list_1__item_f__term_1">vegetation</span> and has a non-combustible, firm and level base.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_113__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When the quantity of flammable and combustible liquids to be stored is more than 100 litres of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-class" id="sec_113__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_6__term_1">class</span> l and/ or more than 210 litres of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-class" id="sec_113__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_6__term_2">class</span> ll and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-class" id="sec_113__subsec_6__term_3" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_6__term_3">class</span> lll A combined, such     flammable and combustible liquids must be stored in a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-store_room" id="sec_113__subsec_6__term_4" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_6__term_4">store room</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_113__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_113__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1), (2), (3), (4) and (6) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_10" data-eId="chp_10"><h2>Chapter 10<br>Transport, supply and delivery of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="chp_10__term_1" data-eId="chp_10__term_1">dangerous goods</span>
</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_114" data-eId="sec_114"><h3>114. Transport of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_114__term_1" data-eId="sec_114__term_1">dangerous goods</span> prohibited without transport <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_114__term_2" data-eId="sec_114__term_2">service</span> permits</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_114__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_114__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_114__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_114__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_114__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_114__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">owner</span> of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_114__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_114__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">vehicle</span> used for transporting <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_114__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_114__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">dangerous goods</span>, must</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_114__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_114__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">be in possession of a valid transport permit issued in accordance with the relevant sections of this bylaw; and ensure that the transport <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_114__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_114__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">service</span> permit is available in          the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_114__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_114__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">vehicle</span> for inspection at all times.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_114__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_114__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_115" data-eId="sec_115"><h3>115. Application for transport <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_115__term_1" data-eId="sec_115__term_1">service</span> permits</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_115__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_115__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An application for a transport permit must be completed and submitted to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_115__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_115__subsec_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span> in the form and manner <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed" id="sec_115__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_115__subsec_1__term_2">prescribed</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_115__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_115__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The application form must be accompanied by proof of payment as <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed" id="sec_115__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_115__subsec_2__term_1">prescribed</span> in the municipal tariff policy.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_116" data-eId="sec_116"><h3>116. Requirements of transport <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_116__term_1" data-eId="sec_116__term_1">service</span> permits</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_116__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_116__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A transport permit</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">may not be issued by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">chief fire officer</span> for a period longer than 12months; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">must</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">indicate the date of issue and expiry;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">identify the issuing officer and bear that officers signature;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">contain a serial number;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">indicate the group and quantity of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iv__term_1" data-eId="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iv__term_1">dangerous goods</span> that may be transported under the permit; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_v" data-eId="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">contain a description of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_v__term_1" data-eId="sec_116__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_v__term_1">vehicle</span> concerned, including its registration number.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_117" data-eId="sec_117"><h3>117. Cancellation of transport <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_117__term_1" data-eId="sec_117__term_1">service</span> permit</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_117__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_117__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The provisions of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_44" href="#sec_44">section 44</a>, read with the necessary changes, apply to any cancellation of a transport permit by the chief fire officer.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_118" data-eId="sec_118"><h3>118. Exemption from transport <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_118__term_1" data-eId="sec_118__term_1">service</span> permits</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_118__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_118__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A transport <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_118__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_118__hcontainer_1__term_1">service</span> permit contemplated in section 100 is not required for the transportation of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_118__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_118__hcontainer_1__term_2">dangerous goods</span> of the type and not exceeding the quantities stipulated in Schedule 3.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_119" data-eId="sec_119"><h3>119. Design, construction, maintenance and repair of road tankers</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_119__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_119__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every person who designs, constructs, maintains or repairs any road tanker for the transportation of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">dangerous goods</span> must</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">comply with the provisions of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">SANS</span> 0189, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">SANS</span> 1398, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_3">SANS</span> 0233, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_4" data-eId="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_4">SANS</span> 087, Part 6 <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_5" data-eId="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_5">SANS</span> 089, Part 1, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_6" data-eId="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_6">SANS</span> 0230 and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_7" data-eId="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_7">SANS</span> 1518, as the case may be; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">ensure that the road tanker is labelled in a manner that complies with the provisions of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_119__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">SANS</span> 0232 and any applicable law.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_119__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_119__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_120" data-eId="sec_120"><h3>120. containers;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_120__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_120__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_120__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii__term_1" data-eId="sec_120__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii__term_1">SANS</span> 314;</span></span><span static-free wheel blocks;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_120__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_v" data-eId="sec_120__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_v"><span
