transit.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_120__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_120__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_121" data-eId="sec_121"><h3>121. General prohibitions regarding transport of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_121__term_1" data-eId="sec_121__term_1">dangerous goods</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_121__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No person may <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">use</span> or allow to be used, any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">vehicle</span> to transport <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">dangerous goods</span>, unless</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">vehicle</span> has a valid roadworthy certificate;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">if not exempt in terms of section 104, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_1">vehicle</span> is equipped with at least two 9 kilogram dry chemical fire extinguishers</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">designed and manufactured in accordance with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_1">SANS</span> 810 and maintained in accordance with <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_2" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_2">SANS</span> 0105 and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_3" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_3">SANS</span> 1475; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">positioned and installed so that there is at least one <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-fire_extinguisher" id="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1">fire extinguisher</span> on each side of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_2" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_2">vehicle</span> that can be reached quickly and easily in the event of a fire.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_121__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-use" id="sec_121__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_2__term_1">use</span> or allow to be used any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_121__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_2__term_2">vehicle</span> to transport <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_121__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_2__term_3">dangerous goods</span> unless the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_121__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_2__term_4">vehicle</span> cabin, body, cargo space, cargo tank, fuel tank, chassis and engine are         effectively and permanently earthed with each other.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_121__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may cause any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_121__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_3__term_1">vehicle</span> transporting <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_121__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_3__term_2">dangerous goods</span> to travel or overnight in any area where such travel or overnighting is specifically prohibited.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_121__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_121__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1) and (2) and (3) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_122" data-eId="sec_122"><h3>122. Supply of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_122__term_1" data-eId="sec_122__term_1">dangerous goods</span> prohibited in certain circumstances</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_122__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may deliver or supply or allow to be delivered or supplied any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_122__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_1__term_1">dangerous goods</span> of a type and in a quantity exceeding that specified in Schedule 2 to any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_122__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_1__term_2">premises</span>       that are not registered as contemplated in section 63(1).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_122__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may deliver or supply or allow to be delivered or supplied any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_122__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_2__term_1">dangerous goods</span> to any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_122__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_2__term_2">premises</span> in contravention of any conditions of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-certificate_of_registration" id="sec_122__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_2__term_3">certificate of registration</span>     applicable to those <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_122__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_2__term_4">premises</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_122__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may handle or allow to be handled any container containing <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_122__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_3__term_1">dangerous goods</span> in a manner that may damage that container.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_122__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every person who delivers <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__term_1">dangerous goods</span> must ensure that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a 9 kilogram dry chemical fire-extinguisher is available at all times during the delivery;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">during any transfer of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1">dangerous goods</span>, the delivery <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_2">vehicle</span> is physically earthed to the storage facility to which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_3">dangerous goods</span> are being transferred;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">while delivering</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the delivery <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__term_1">vehicle</span> is placed in such a position that it can be moved easily and quickly in the event of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__term_2" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__term_2">emergency</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">the delivery <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__term_1">vehicle</span> is not parked on or across a pavement or a road;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">no delivery hose lies on or across a pavement, road or other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii__term_1" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii__term_1">premises</span>;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">no <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__term_1">dangerous goods</span> are transferred to a storage facility that does not comply with the requirements of Chapter 9 of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__term_2">this by-law</span> and the provisions of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-SANS" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__term_3" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__term_3">SANS</span> 0263;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_e__list_1" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_e__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">any device connected with, or used for, the delivery of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_1">dangerous goods</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">is designed for its purpose; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">is maintained in safe and good working condition; and</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">no <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_4__list_1__item_f__term_1">dangerous goods</span> are spilled during delivery.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_122__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may transfer or allow to be transferred any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_122__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_5__term_1">dangerous goods</span> to any motor <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_122__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_5__term_2">vehicle</span>, aircraft, vessel, ship or boat while its power source is in operation.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_122__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No person may transfer any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dangerous_goods" id="sec_122__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_6__term_1">dangerous goods</span> to any aircraft unless the aircraft is earthed to the transferral device by means of an earth cable.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_122__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_122__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsections (1), (2), (3), (4), (5) and (6) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_123" data-eId="sec_123"><h3>123. Records of transport permits</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_123__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_123__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_123__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_123__hcontainer_1__term_1">chief fire officer</span> must keep updated records of all vehicles in respect of which a transport permit has been issued, amended or renewed.</span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_11" data-eId="chp_11"><h2>Chapter 11<br>Spray painting and spraying rooms</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_124" data-eId="sec_124"><h3>124. Spray rooms and booths</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_124__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_124__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-spray" id="sec_124__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_124__hcontainer_1__term_1">spray</span> room, booth or area designated for the application of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_liquid" id="sec_124__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_124__hcontainer_1__term_2">flammable liquid</span> must be constructed and equipped according to the requirements in Schedule 4 of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_124__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_124__hcontainer_1__term_3">this by-law</span> and must be operated in such a manner as to comply with the General Safety Regulations promulgated in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Occupational_Health_and_Safety_Act" id="sec_124__hcontainer_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_124__hcontainer_1__term_4">Occupational Health and Safety Act</span>.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_125" data-eId="sec_125"><h3>125. Spraying prohibited without <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-spraying_permit" id="sec_125__term_1" data-eId="sec_125__term_1">spraying permit</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_125__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">No person may <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-spray" id="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">spray</span>, coat, plate or epoxy-coat any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vehicle" id="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">vehicle</span>, article, object or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">building</span> or part thereof or allow them to be sprayed, coated, plated or epoxy-coated with any      <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-flammable_substance" id="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__term_4">flammable substance</span> unless</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">that person is in possession of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-spraying_permit" id="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">spraying permit</span> contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_112" href="#sec_112">section 112</a>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the spraying, coating, plating or epoxy-coating as the case may be is conducted in a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-spraying_room" id="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">spraying room</span> <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approved" id="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">approved</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_3">chief fire officer</span> on <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_4" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_4">premises</span> registered for that             purpose.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_125__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_125__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who contravenes subsection (1) commits an offence.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_126" data-eId="sec_126"><h3>126. Application for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-spraying_permit" id="sec_126__term_1" data-eId="sec_126__term_1">spraying permit</span>
</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_126__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_126__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person who wishes to obtain a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-spraying_permit" id="sec_126__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_126__hcontainer_1__term_1">spraying permit</span> must complete and submit to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_126__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_126__hcontainer_1__term_2">chief fire officer</span> an application form for such permit in the form and manner as <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed" id="sec_126__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_126__hcontainer_1__term_3">prescribed</span>.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_127" data-eId="sec_127"><h3>127. Cancellation of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-spraying_permit" id="sec_127__term_1" data-eId="sec_127__term_1">spraying permit</span>
</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_127__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_127__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The provisions of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_44" href="#sec_44">section 44</a>, read with the necessary changes, apply to the cancellation by the chief fire officer of any spraying permit.</span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_12" data-eId="chp_12"><h2>Chapter 12<br>Miscellaneous</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_128" data-eId="sec_128"><h3>128. Handling of animals during emergencies</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_128__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_128__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_1__term_1">owner</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupier" id="sec_128__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_1__term_2">occupier</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_128__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_1__term_3">person in charge</span> of any zoological garden, feedlot, stable, research institution, veterinary practice or any place of veterinary science study, must       ensure the professional handling of any animal on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_128__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_1__term_4">premises</span> concerned during an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_128__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_1__term_5">emergency</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_128__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding the provisions of subsection (1), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-chief_fire_officer" id="sec_128__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_2__term_1">chief fire officer</span> may, in respect of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_128__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_2__term_2">premises</span>, authorise a suitably qualified person to handle or put down any         animal during an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_128__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_2__term_3">emergency</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_128__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_128__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_3__term_1">municipality</span> may recover any costs incurred in relation to the professional handling or putting down of any animal during an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-emergency" id="sec_128__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_3__term_2">emergency</span> from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_128__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_3__term_3">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person_in_charge" id="sec_128__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_3__term_4">person in charge</span>     of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_128__subsec_3__term_5" data-eId="sec_128__subsec_3__term_5">premises</span> concerned.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_129" data-eId="sec_129"><h3>129. Exemption from provisions of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_129__term_1" data-eId="sec_129__term_1">this by-law</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_129__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_129__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any person may make application to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_129__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_129__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> in writing, for an exemption from any provision of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_129__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_129__subsec_1__term_2">this by-law</span>, specifying the reasons for exemption in such application.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_129__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_129__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_129__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_129__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_129__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_129__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may grant an exemption</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_129__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_129__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">in general or in particular;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_129__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_129__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">for any period; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_129__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_129__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">subject to any condition that will provide the same overall fire prevention and protection that would result from the full application of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_129__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_129__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">this by-law</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_129__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_129__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an exemption is granted in terms of subsection (2), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_129__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_129__subsec_3__term_1">municipality</span> must issue a certificate of exemption to the person concerned, specifying the scope and period of the     exemption and any condition imposed.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_129__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_129__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_129__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_129__subsec_4__term_1">municipality</span> may amend or withdraw a certificate of exemption at any time.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_129__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_129__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The holder of a certificate of exemption must ensure that the certificate is available on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_129__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_129__subsec_5__term_1">premises</span> concerned at all times for inspection by any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-member" id="sec_129__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_129__subsec_5__term_2">member</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_130" data-eId="sec_130"><h3>130. Approval, authorisation or permission under <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_130__term_1" data-eId="sec_130__term_1">this by-law</span>
</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_130__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_130__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_130__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_130__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any person who requires any approval, authorisation or permission contemplated in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_130__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_130__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">this by-law</span> in respect of which no application procedure is provided, must apply for that approval, authorisation or permission</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_130__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_130__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">by completing and submitting an application in the form and manner determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_130__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_130__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">municipality</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_130__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_130__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">by paying the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-prescribed" id="sec_130__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_130__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">prescribed</span> tariff.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_131" data-eId="sec_131"><h3>131. Cancellation of approval, authorisation or permission</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_131__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_131__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The provisions of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_44" href="#sec_44">section 44</a>, read with the necessary changes, apply to any approval, authorisation or permission contemplated in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_116" href="#sec_116">section 116</a>.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_132" data-eId="sec_132"><h3>132. By-law binds <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-State" id="sec_132__term_1" data-eId="sec_132__term_1">State</span>
</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_132__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_132__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">This by-law binds the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-State" id="sec_132__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_132__hcontainer_1__term_1">State</span> and any person in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-service" id="sec_132__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_132__hcontainer_1__term_2">service</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-State" id="sec_132__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_132__hcontainer_1__term_3">State</span>.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_133" data-eId="sec_133"><h3>133. Conflict with other legislation</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_133__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_133__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In the event of any conflict between any provision of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_133__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_133__hcontainer_1__term_1">this by-law</span> and National and Provincial legislation, standards, policies or guidelines, the National and Provincial legislation, standards, policies or guidelines shall prevail.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_134" data-eId="sec_134"><h3>134. Offences and penalties</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_134__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_134__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_134__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_134__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A person who contravenes any provision or fails to comply with any provision of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_134__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_134__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">this by-law</span> commits an offence and shall on conviction be liable to</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_134__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_134__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a fine or imprisonment, or either such fine or imprisonment or to both such fine and such imprisonment and,</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_134__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_134__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of a continuing offence, to an additional fine or an additional period of imprisonment or to such additional imprisonment without the option of a fine or to          both such additional fine and imprisonment for each day on which such offence is continued and,</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_134__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_134__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">a further amount equal to any costs and expenses found by the court to have been incurred by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_134__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_134__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">municipality</span> as result of such contravention or failure.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_135" data-eId="sec_135"><h3>135. Repeal of by-laws</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_135__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_135__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The provisions of any by-laws previously promulgated by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_135__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_135__hcontainer_1__term_1">municipality</span> or by any of the disestablished municipalities now incorporated in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_135__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_135__hcontainer_1__term_2">municipality</span>, are hereby repealed as far as they relate to matters provided for in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-this_by_law" id="sec_135__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_135__hcontainer_1__term_3">this by-law</span>, and insofar as it has been made applicable to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_135__hcontainer_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_135__hcontainer_1__term_4">municipality</span> by the authorisation for the execution of powers and functions in terms of section 84(3) of the Local Government: Municipal Structures Act, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1998/117" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1998/117">Act 117 of 1998</a>.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_136" data-eId="sec_136"><h3>136. Short title and commencement</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_136__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_136__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">This by-law shall be known as the Fire Safety By-law and comes into operation on the date of publication in the Provincial Gazette.</span></span></span></section></section></span><span class="akn-attachments"><div class="akn-attachment" id="att_1" data-eId="att_1">
<h2 class="akn-heading">Schedule 1</h2>
<h2 class="akn-subheading">Guideline for emergency evacuation plans</h2>
<span class="akn-doc" data-name="schedule"><span class="akn-mainBody"><section class="akn-section" id="att_1/sec_137" data-eId="sec_137"><h3>137. Content of emergency evacuation plans</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="att_1/sec_137__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_137__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every emergency evacuation plan contemplated in section 37 must contain at least the information under the headings below.</span></span></span><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_1/sec_137__subsec_1" telephone numbers.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_1/sec_137__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_137__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span premises;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/sec_137__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_137__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the number of persons present on the premises at any time;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/sec_137__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_137__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">an indication of any control room on the premises;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/sec_137__subsec_2__list_1__item_e" person in the event of an emergency.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_1/sec_137__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_137__subsec_3"><span premises that may be relevant to evacuation in an emergency.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_1/sec_137__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_137__subsec_4"><span emergency.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_1/sec_137__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_137__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span plan; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/sec_137__subsec_10__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_137__subsec_10__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">a bomb threat questionnaire.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="att_1/sec_138" data-eId="sec_138"><h3>138. Review of emergency evacuation plans</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="att_1/sec_138__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_138__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An emergency evacuation plan must be reviewed and updated by the owner or occupier of the premises concerned at least once each year and whenever a member of the management of the emergency team ceases to work at the premises.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_1/sec_138__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_138__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Whenever an emergency evacuation plan is reviewed and updated, the owner or occupier of the premises concerned must ensure that all old plans on the premises or in the possession of the management of the emergency team are collected and destroyed in order to eliminate any confusion regarding the validity and accuracy of the evacuation plan.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="att_1/sec_139" data-eId="sec_139"><h3>139. Emergency evacuation drills</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="att_1/sec_139__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_139__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An emergency evacuation plan should be drilled at least twice each year and involve the participation of all persons who work or reside in the building concerned.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_1/sec_139__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_139__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The owner or person in charge of a building should give all persons who are to be involved in an emergency evacuation drill at least 21 days notice of the drill.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="att_1/sec_140" data-eId="sec_140"><h3>140. Emergency evacuation awareness</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="att_1/sec_140__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_140__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every person who works or resides on premises should be aware of the emergency evacuation plan for that premises.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="att_1/sec_141" data-eId="sec_141"><h3>141. Training of persons</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="att_1/sec_141__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_141__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_1/sec_141__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_141__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every person who resides or works on premises with an emergency evacuation plan should be suitably trained in</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/sec_141__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_141__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">first aid or fire fighting;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/sec_141__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_141__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">emergency aid;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/sec_141__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_141__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">emergency evacuation procedures; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_1/sec_141__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_141__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">emergency management techniques.</span></span></span></span></span></section></span></span>
</div>
<div class="akn-attachment" id="att_2" data-eId="att_2">
<h2 class="akn-heading">Schedule 2</h2>
<h2 class="akn-subheading">Exemption from certificate of registration</h2>
<span class="akn-doc" data-name="schedule"><span class="akn-mainBody"><span class="akn-paragraph" id="att_2/para_142" data-eId="para_142"><span class="akn-num">142.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A certificate of registration is in terms of section 67(2) not required if the flammable substances concerned are of a type and do not exceed the quantity stipulated below.</span><table id="att_2/para_142__table_1" data-eId="para_142__table_1">
<tr><th colspan="3" class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">Gases:</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td rowspan="3" class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">Class O</span></td>
<td rowspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Liquefied petroleum gas</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Flat: Total cylinder capacity may not exceed 9 kg per flat.</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><td><span class="akn-p">Houses or commercial premises: Total maximum of 19 kg inside and total maximum of 100 kg on premises.</span></td></tr>
<tr><td><span class="akn-p">Industrial premises: Maximum of 19 kg per 600m of building space with a total maximum of 100 kg.</span></td></tr>
<tr><th colspan="3" class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">Flammable liquids and combustible liquids:</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">Class I</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Liquids that have a closed-cap flash point of below 38 C</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Total maximum of 40 litres</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">Class II</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Liquids that have a closed-cap flash point of 38 C or above, but below 60,5 C</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Total quantity of Class II and Class IIIA together may not exceed the maximum quantity of 210 litres</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">Class IIIA</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Liquids that have a close-cap flash point of 60,5 C or above but below 93 C</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"></span></td>
</tr>
</table></span></span></span></span>
</div>
<div class="akn-attachment" id="att_3" data-eId="att_3">
<h2 class="akn-heading">Schedule 3</h2>
<h2 class="akn-subheading">Exemption from transport permit</h2>
<span class="akn-doc" data-name="schedule"><span class="akn-mainBody"><span class="akn-paragraph" id="att_3/para_143" data-eId="para_143"><span class="akn-num">143.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A transport permit is in terms of section 100 not required for the transport of dangerous goods of the type and not exceeding the quantity stipulated below.</span><table id="att_3/para_143__table_1" data-eId="para_143__table_1">
<tr>
<th><span class="akn-p">GROUP</span></th>
<th><span class="akn-p">DESCRIPTION</span></th>
<th><span class="akn-p">QUANTITY</span></th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">II</span></td>
<td colspan="2"><span class="akn-p">GASES</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Flammable gases</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Total cylinder capacity may not exceed 50 kilograms</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Non-flammable gases</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Total cylinder capacity may not exceed 333 kilograms</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">III</span></td>
<td colspan="2"><span class="akn-p">FLAMMABLE LIQUIDS</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">With flash points &gt; 18 C</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Total quantity may not exceed 100 litres</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">With flash points &gt; 18 C but  23 C</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Total quantity may not exceed 420 litres</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">With flash points &gt; 23 C but  61 C</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Total quantity may not exceed 1100 litres</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">With flash points &gt; 61 C but  100 C</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Total quantity may not exceed 1100 litres</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">IV</span></td>

</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"></span></td>

</tr>
<tr>

<tr>

</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Group II organic peroxides in packets</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Total quantity may not exceed 200 kilograms</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>

<tr>

</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Group II toxic substances in packets</span></td>

</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"></span></td>

<div class="akn-attachment" id="att_4" data-eId="att_4">
<h2 class="akn-heading">Schedule 4</h2>
<h2 class="akn-subheading">Spray booth construction</h2>
<span class="akn-doc" data-name="schedule"><span class="akn-mainBody"><span class="akn-hcontainer" id="att_4/hcontainer_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><table id="att_4/hcontainer_1__table_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__table_1">
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">WALLS</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">225 mm Brickwork.</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">ROOF</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Reinforced concrete.</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">FLOOR</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Concrete or other impervious material.</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">DOORS (A)</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Constructed of 50 mm hardwood completely covered, including the edges, with 24 s.w.g. metal secured to the door with bolts at 30 mm centres along the edges. The doors to open outwards and to be hung on Tee hinges bolted to the door.</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">(B)</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Close fitting metal doors not lees than 3 mm in thickness, carried on an angle iron frame and having an all round overlap or not less than 50 mm.</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">NOTE:</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Where the floor area exceeds 18 sq. metres 2 doors must be provided.</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">WINDOWS</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Metal frames with no opening sections glazed with wire-woven glass not exceeding 460mm  460 mm. Putty approved by the SANS Code No. 680/59 only to be used and the occupier to furnish proof of this to the Director: Fire and Emergency Services.</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">NOTE:</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">The Factory Inspector requires natural light to the extend of 20% of the floor area.</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">VENTILATION</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">30 Lineal metres/minute velocity across the room must be provided by means of mechanical ventilation, with the centre line of the inlets 460mm above the floor level and to discharge through vertical metal ducting terminating one (1) metre above the apex of the roof. No right angle bends to be used in the ducting system. Exhaust fans to be installed at four (4) metre centres or horizontal metal ducting extending the entire length of the wall with suitable inlets, must be provided.</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">NOTE:</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">If the ducting is external to the Spray Booth and in communication with the Workshop etc., it must be protected by either 110mm brick or 50mm asbestos cement lagging.</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">VENTILATION INLETS</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">The wall opposite the exhaust fans to be honeycombed with airbricks installed from 100mm above floor level to a height of not less than two (2) metres.</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">MINIMUM NO. OF AIRBRICKS</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">SIZE OF ROOM</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">40</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Up to but not exceeding 140 cubic meters</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">65</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Up to but not exceeding 280 cubic meters</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">90</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Up to but not exceeding 470 cubic meters</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">150</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Up to but not exceeding 650 cubic meters</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><td colspan="2"><span class="akn-p">NOTE: Metal filters with metal swarf elements may only be used in an all metal installation, in lieu of Airbricks.</span></td></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">ELECTRICAL WORK</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">All electrical work must be of flame-proof construction.</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">DANGER NOTICE</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">"DANGER  NO SMOKING" notices in 150mm high white letters on a red background to be provided above the doors outside the Spray Booth.</span></td>
</tr>
</table></span></span></span></span>
</div></span></article></span>





</div>
